:   "*Size matters not. Look at me. Judge me by my size, do you? Hmm? Hmm. And well you should not. For my ally is the Force, and a powerful ally it is. Life creates it, makes it grow. Its energy surrounds us and binds us. Luminous beings are we, not this crude matter. You must feel the Force around you; here, between you, me, the tree, the rock, everywhere, yes. Even between the land and the ship.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Luke Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Yoda-SizeMattersNot-Full.flac/revision/latest?cb=20251220050900)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Yoda-SizeMattersNot-Full.flac "File:Yoda-SizeMattersNot-Full.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7)

**Yoda** was a legendary [Jedi Grand Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") who led the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") through the time of the High Republic, in the years leading up to its destruction by the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"), and during the transformation of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Small in stature but revered for his wisdom and power, Yoda trained generations of [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), ultimately serving as the Jedi Order's [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master"). He played integral roles in defending the Republic during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), survived Order 66, and lived to pass on the Jedi tradition to [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), and unlocking the path to [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality").

[Born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in [896 BBY](/wiki/896_BBY "896 BBY"), Yoda served the Jedi Order for [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century"), becoming Jedi [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") and helping to teach many [younglings](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate"). During the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), in [382 BBY](/wiki/382_BBY "382 BBY"), Yoda helped bring an end to a devastating battle between the Jedi and the [anti-Jedi](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment") [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") [cult](/wiki/Religion "Religion"). After the battle, which became known as the [Night of Sorrow](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow"), he decided to keep the living weapons against [Force-sensitives](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") the Path had used, the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai"), out of the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") to protect the order. Over a century later, he took a sabbatical from the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") to train [Padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") aboard the *[Star Hopper](/wiki/Star_Hopper "Star Hopper")*, leading them and other Jedi in fighting the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") organization in [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY"). After disappearing without explanation for over a year, Yoda reappeared in [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY "230 BBY") on [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia"), where he helped his former Padawan [Kantam Sy](/wiki/Kantam_Sy "Kantam Sy") and other Jedi [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Corellian_Shipyards "Battle of the Corellian Shipyards") the Nihil, accompanied by a former Jedi who fought in the Night of Sorrow named [Azlin Rell](/wiki/Azlin_Rell "Azlin Rell"). As the Nihil had also weaponized the Nameless, Yoda hoped that Rell's knowledge he had accrued about the creatures since the battle would help the Jedi find a way to fight them.

Yoda was almost nine hundred [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") old in the latter [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") of the Republic. A leading member of the Jedi High Council, his contemporaries included other legendary Masters, such as [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") and [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi"). During the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"), in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"), the maverick [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") introduced [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") to the High Council, believing with absolute certainty that he had discovered the prophesied [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"). The Jedi elders sensed that the [boy](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") was full of fear and anger and declined to train him, deeming Skywalker too old and emotionally compromised to commit himself to the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code"). After Jinn's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") during the [liberation](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"), the High Council reversed their decision in spite of Yoda's continued opposition to Skywalker's apprenticeship, having sensed grave danger in his training. At the same [time](/wiki/Time "Time"), the Jedi discovered that their [ancient nemesis](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War"), the Sith, had returned after a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") in hiding. Aware of the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"), Yoda was convinced that at least one more [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") remained active following [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi")'s victory over the [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul").

Over the next decade, [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") was on the verge of civil war with entire [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system")—led by [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), Yoda's one-time Padawan—threatening to [secede](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") from the Republic by [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). Unable to defend the entire Republic against this betrayal on their own, the Jedi took command of the newly-formed [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"), with Yoda himself leading an [army](/wiki/Army "Army") of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") against the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") in the [first battle](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") of the [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Wars, rescuing the Jedi and Senator from execution. For three years Yoda led the [Republic military's](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") war effort as a [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General"), determined to bring a swift and decisive end to the conflict. During this time he was approached by the spirit of Qui-Gon Jinn, who helped Yoda learn how to retain his identity as a [spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") after death. Yoda's efforts against the Separatists were undermined by [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") who [conspired](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") to [destroy the Jedi](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") and [restore the Sith](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") to power. After the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") commenced in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), killing thousands of Jedi both on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") and across the galaxy, Yoda [confronted](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Galactic_Senate "Duel in the Galactic Senate") the [self-declared](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") but failed to cut short Sidious' reign and consequently retreated into [exile](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)"), leaving the [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") to consolidate his power with a new apprentice, the former Anakin Skywalker-turned-[Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader, at his side.

Yoda's remaining years were spent living in [isolation](/wiki/Hermit "Hermit") on the remote world of [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah"). After the death of Obi-Wan Kenobi, he was able to commune with his spirit, who wished for Yoda to train Anakin's [son](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"). Yoda initially reluctantly agreed, but later believed that the galaxy as better off without him and refused Kenobi's request. After being convinced by Kenobi to enter the [Cave of Evil](/wiki/Cave_of_Evil "Cave of Evil"), in which he confronted many figures from his past and made peace with his failures, he agreed to teach Luke Skywalker, who soon after sought out the legendary Grand Master in the hope of becoming a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"). He trained Skywalker for a time, until despite Yoda's warnings Skywalker hurriedly abandoned his training to save his friends after a having a vision that they were in danger. A year later, in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"), with his health rapidly declining, Yoda died of old age when Skywalker returned to see him. He became [one with the Force](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit"), shortly before Luke redeemed his father Anakin, who fulfilled his destiny as the Chosen One by killing Sidious.

Years later, Luke Skywalker's attempt to reform the Jedi Order would be foiled when his nephew [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") turned to the dark side and destroyed his [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker"). Believing the galaxy was better without him and the Jedi, Skywalker went into exile, just as Yoda had. After his student he reluctantly trained, the [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), also abandoned her training, Yoda appeared as a ghost to Skywalker. Yoda taught Skywalker to learn from his failures and helped him forgive himself.

## Biography

### Early life

:   "*For 800 years have I trained Jedi.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Luke Skywalker[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7)

[Born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") [nine-hundred](/wiki/896_BBY "896 BBY") [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"),[[19]](#cite_note-BioGal17-19) Yoda belonged to an ancient and mysterious [species](/wiki/Yoda%27s_species "Yoda's species")[[4]](#cite_note-Card_Trader-4) and little was known of Yoda's early life;[[20]](#cite_note-USWNE-20) he never revealed [his homeworld](/wiki/Yoda%27s_homeworld "Yoda's homeworld").[[1]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-1) As he was [keenly attuned](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") to [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"), he joined the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") as a [youngling](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling"). After undergoing the ritual known as [the Gathering](/wiki/Gathering "Gathering"), he received his [kyber crystal](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal"), and [Professor](/wiki/Professor "Professor") [Huyang](/wiki/Huyang "Huyang") helped him construct his first [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber") aboard the *[Crucible](/wiki/Crucible "Crucible")*.[[21]](#cite_note-ANB-21)[[22]](#cite_note-AToS-22) At some point during his [time](/wiki/Time "Time") as a youngling, Yoda skipped across the lily pads in the [Jedi Grand Temple's](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") meditation pond.[[23]](#cite_note-L&D-23)

Although Yoda spoke little of his early days, it was rumored that one of his early [instructors](/wiki/Teacher "Teacher") was the [Hysalrian](/wiki/Hysalrian "Hysalrian") [N'Kata Del Gormo](/wiki/N%27Kata_Del_Gormo "N'Kata Del Gormo").[[11]](#cite_note-The_Glass_Abyss-11) Yoda was paired up with a personal [mentor](/wiki/Yoda%27s_old_Master "Yoda's old Master"). During their time together, Yoda's [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") told him the tale of [K'ungfu](/wiki/K%27ungfu "K'ungfu") and [Chuang](/wiki/Chuang "Chuang"), two great [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") of the past.[[6]](#cite_note-SYWtBaJ?-6) Around the age of 100, in [796 BBY](/wiki/796_BBY "796 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Yoda was ready to pass on what he had learned. Having attained the rank of Master, he spent the next eight centuries training and tutoring generations of Jedi.[[5]](#cite_note-DatabankYoda-5) It was estimated that over his lifetime, he trained around twenty-thousand Jedi.[[24]](#cite_note-AEYNK-24)

### High Republic Era

#### Early High Republic Era

:   "*You must choose the Force. One does not fall into being a Jedi Knight by mistake, hm? Or because it is convenient! You must choose the Force, with your whole heart. To do this, you must learn, again, to listen. To hear the world, the world outside of your own emotions. Even when they are very, very loud, heh,* [like] *a hurricane.*"
:   ―Yoda[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

By the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), Yoda was considered a great Jedi Master. He had also gained a seat on the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council")[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26) and the rank of [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master").[[27]](#cite_note-THR_1-27) Two other Jedi—[Xo Lahru](/wiki/Xo_Lahru "Xo Lahru") and [Pra-Tre Veter](/wiki/Pra-Tre_Veter "Pra-Tre Veter")—shared the Grand Master title with Yoda.[[28]](#cite_note-Jedi_Council_Revealed-28) Eventually the [human](/wiki/Human "Human") Jedi [Ry Ki-Sakka](/wiki/Ry_Ki-Sakka "Ry Ki-Sakka") also attained the position.[[29]](#cite_note-THRS_4-29) As the Jedi who taught younglings, Yoda one day met the human youngling [Gella Nattai](/wiki/Gella_Nattai "Gella Nattai"), who was scared of the [training remotes](/wiki/Marksman-H_training_remote "Marksman-H training remote") and ran from the room. Finding Nattai in the Temple garden and sitting with her, Yoda and Nattai watched a frog in the garden repeatedly try to jump into a waterfall behind a stone wall. Yoda used the frog as a lesson, teaching her to face her fear and always get back up to try again.[[30]](#cite_note-Convergence-30)

#### An uncertain Path

:   "*No one, no galaxy, no Republic, no Jedi Order, no family, is perfect.*"  
    "*You are right. […] Perhaps we are doing too much, too fast.*"  
    "*You must continue. The great good is a good vision. Fight for this good as well, the Jedi do.*"
:   ―Yoda and Chancellor Kyong Greylark[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

 [![The Path of the Open Hand](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PathOfTheOpenHandMembersSymbol-CharactersOfSWTHR.png/revision/latest?cb=20221021134015) [![The Path of the Open Hand](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PathOfTheOpenHandMembersSymbol-CharactersOfSWTHR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221021134015)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PathOfTheOpenHandMembersSymbol-CharactersOfSWTHR.png/revision/latest?cb=20221021134015) 

The Path of the Open Hand

 

In [382 BBY](/wiki/382_BBY "382 BBY"), after learning of the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha") and the failure of a [peace treaty](/wiki/Eiram%E2%80%93E%27ronoh_peace_treaty "Eiram–E'ronoh peace treaty") between the [warring](/wiki/Eiram_and_E%27ronoh_War "Eiram and E'ronoh War") planets [Eiram](/wiki/Eiram "Eiram") and [E'ronoh](/wiki/E%27ronoh "E'ronoh") there, Yoda went to the [Republic Executive Building](/wiki/Imperial_Executive_Building "Imperial Executive Building") on the galactic capital [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") to meet with with [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Kyong Greylark](/wiki/Kyong_Greylark "Kyong Greylark") while they waited for more information from [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha"). They spoke to Jedi Master [Creighton Sun](/wiki/Creighton_Sun "Creighton Sun") and [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Aida Forte](/wiki/Aida_Forte "Aida Forte"), who were on the ground on Jedha and confirmed that the E'roni ambassador was dead and the Eirami had deployed a droid army. They requested to perform an investigation on the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") planet [Dalna](/wiki/Dalna "Dalna") of the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") cult, considering their involvement in the failure of the peace talks, the fact that Jedi Master [Silandra Sho](/wiki/Silandra_Sho "Silandra Sho") felt a disturbance that made the Jedi ill at the Path's [almshouse](/wiki/Healing_house "Healing house"), and that Jedi Knight Gella Nattai believed the Chancellor's criminal son [Axel Greylark](/wiki/Axel_Greylark "Axel Greylark") was working with the Path. Yoda admitted that he had sensed a disturbance beyond Jedha, and emphasized that they need to be careful, reminding them that there was always those who thrived in chaos. After much deliberation, Yoda and Chancellor Greylark eventually agreed to a fact-finding mission accompanied by two of her guards and to send Jedi Master [Char-Ryl-Roy](/wiki/Char-Ryl-Roy "Char-Ryl-Roy") and [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Enya Keen](/wiki/Enya_Keen "Enya Keen") to Eiram and E'ronoh to try and keep the peace and discover what was causing [communications buoys](/wiki/Communications_buoy "Communications buoy") to be down, Yoda explaining to them that [Werth Plouth](/wiki/Werth_Plouth "Werth Plouth"), the Path's [Herald](/wiki/Herald_(title) "Herald (title)"), was responsible for the riots on Jedha.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

After the communication ended, Yoda expressed his concern as they received another message from Jedi Master [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle"), who was accompanied by a [Jedi Initiate](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate") named [Cippa Tarko](/wiki/Cippa_Tarko "Cippa Tarko"), though the connection of the message was poor. Tarko asked about Yoda, and Yaddle explained that he was a Jedi Master and not her brother. Yoda told Yaddle that they were sending help to Jedha and two Jedi to Dalna and that she was to return to Coruscant, but the message was so choppy they were not sure if she understood. Yoda had an unsettling feeling in the Force that reminded him of the feeling he got whenever a battle was coming. Master Yaddle did misunderstand Yoda's message to mean she was needed on Dalna and joined Sun and Forte there, who sent a message to Yoda confirming they were there shortly before Yaddle arrived.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

 [![Jedi Master Yaddle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/Yaddle-SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20241228210308) [![Jedi Master Yaddle](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/Yaddle-SWCT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20241228210308)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/Yaddle-SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20241228210308) 

Jedi Master Yaddle

 

Later, Chancellor Greylark had her guards summon Yoda to her to reveal that her son Axel had escaped from prison with the help of the Path and someone named [Binnot Ullo](/wiki/Binnot_Ullo "Binnot Ullo"). She told Yoda that she did not know who Ullo was and did not think Axel had many friends. He assured her that no one, no galaxy, and no republic was perfect, and that she should continue to fight for the greater good like the Jedi did. She explained that she felt like they have all been moving through a fog that has corrupted everything lately and Yoda insisted that Axel still had good in him and that the 'fog' was just corrupting him too. However, the Chancellor resolved to make Axel truly feel the consequences of his actions.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

#### Chancellor no more

:   "*We will go together. Chancellor you may not be anymore. Friend, you still are.*"
:   ―Yoda to Greylark, on going to Dalna[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

 [![Chancellor Kyong Greylark](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/KyongGreylark-THRS.png/revision/latest?cb=20250104230422) [![Chancellor Kyong Greylark](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/KyongGreylark-THRS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20250104230422)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/KyongGreylark-THRS.png/revision/latest?cb=20250104230422) 

Chancellor Kyong Greylark

 

Eventually, Greylark received a message from her son on Dalna and immediately called Yoda to have him listen to it with her via hologram. After hearing Axel ask for her to go to Dalna to speak with the Path and with him, Yoda asked her what she would do, the Chancellor deciding to go to Dalna. She then recorded a message for Axel that included Yoda in it, wearing a blank expression, so that he could bear witness to her stepping down as Chancellor. After she sent the message, Yoda stayed with her wordlessly for a while, and she appreciated his kindness.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

Before Greylark could leave for Dalna, Yoda approached her and said that since he had not heard back from Masters Sun or [Ela Sutan](/wiki/Ela_Sutan "Ela Sutan"), who had also been sent to Dalna, that he would go with her because she was still his friend even though she was no longer Chancellor. Yoda had a Jedi [Longbeam cruiser](/wiki/Longbeam-class_corvette "Longbeam-class corvette") follow them with a contingent of Jedi. While in hyperspace, they received a distress call from [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Xiri A'lbaran](/wiki/Xiri_A%27lbaran "Xiri A'lbaran") of E'ronoh and Prince [Phan-tu Zenn](/wiki/Phan-tu_Zenn "Phan-tu Zenn") of Eiram. They then received a message from Chancellor [Orlen Mollo](/wiki/Orlen_Mollo "Orlen Mollo"), who said that the leaders of Eiram and E'ronoh were still not cooperating. Yoda volunteered to rescue the heirs due to their proximity to them and left, taking other Jedi with him.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

#### The Night of Sorrow

:   "*Speak to the Jedi Council soon, you should. We must explain the happenings on Dalna. All that went wrong.*" […]   
    *"But we must also speak to all the things that went right. We could not have defeated the Path without the Jedi.*"  
    "*And the Jedi could not have defeated the Path without the help of our Republic allies.*"
:   ―Yoda and Greylark[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

Eventually, Yoda arrived at the battle that was now raging on Dalna between the Path and the Jedi, which came to be known as the [Night of Sorrow](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow").[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31) The Path, much of it reorganized into the [Path of the Closed Fist](/wiki/Path_of_the_Closed_Fist "Path of the Closed Fist"), was led by [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro") of the [Ro family](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family").[[32]](#cite_note-PoV-32) He was joined by Princess A'lbaran and Prince Zenn, the three announcing that the combined forces of Eiram and E'ronoh were there to fight together with the Jedi. When Yoda arrived on the ground at the [Path compound](/wiki/Path_compound "Path compound"), Jedi Gella Nattai told him to direct people to go to the cave system as there was potentially many more Path members there.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31) On Dalna, he met[[33]](#cite_note-HRA_5-33) Path [Little](/wiki/Littles "Littles")[[32]](#cite_note-PoV-32) [Tromak](/wiki/Tromak "Tromak"). Yoda eventually came to forget Tromak but always remembered the importance of his visit to Dalna.[[33]](#cite_note-HRA_5-33)

 [![The Path's compound on Dalna](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/PathCompound.png/revision/latest?cb=20221017125216) [![The Path's compound on Dalna](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/PathCompound.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221017125216)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/PathCompound.png/revision/latest?cb=20221017125216) 

The Path's compound on Dalna

 

As the battle started to come to a close with it turning in the Jedi's favor, Yoda and Yaddle stood together, the latter watching Cippa Tarko sleep. However, A'lbaran and Zenn contacted them and informed them that explosions have been set off underground. As Yaddle suggested getting help, the ground shook and Yoda spotted sections of the caves collapse into sinkholes. Yoda and Yaddle then sensed a Jedi in distress and went to help. Finding a door in the ground, Yoda and Yaddle connected to the force and sensed Gella Nattai and Axel Greylark. Yaddle lifted up the ground, rocks, and soil while Yoda lifted the water to try and rescue them. Enya Keen then ran toward them, seeing Nattai, and pulled her and Axel from the mud-like water, having been brought to the surface by the two Jedi Masters. Yoda and Yaddle then set the water and mud down far away. In the sinkhole, E'roni and Eirami soldiers began recovering survivors. Yaddle noticed that the sounds of battle have faded and the sun was rising. She asks Yoda if the battle was done, and he says it was.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

Yoda met with Kyong Greylark and Chancellor Mollo on a medical frigate above Coruscant, the three discussing now only having one Chancellor instead of two and what it means. Yoda suggested they speak to the Jedi Council and tell them everything that went wrong, but Greylark also wanted to focus all the things that went right, including the help of the Republic and the Jedi. Mollo revealed that the people of Dalna were calling the event the Night of Sorrow. While he imagined the future, Greylark assured Yoda that she would meet him on Coruscant soon, Yoda adding that there was much to celebrate and remember.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

#### Return to the Temple

:   "*What do you know about these nameless creatures?*"  
    *"I, too, know of them. Powerful beings, they are. Dangerous, they are. But in pain, they could be. Only a few understand them. You, and I. And still, much to learn is there.*"
:   ―Yoda and Creighton Sun[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

 [![One of the Nameless creatures during the Night of Sorrow](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/NightofSorrow.png/revision/latest?cb=20230417143823) [![One of the Nameless creatures during the Night of Sorrow](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/NightofSorrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230417143823)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/NightofSorrow.png/revision/latest?cb=20230417143823) 

One of the Nameless creatures during the Night of Sorrow

 

Yoda then traveled to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on Coruscant, confirming first that the royal families of Eiram and E'ronoh had already gathered, who he met with when he arrived. He met with several Jedi, including Yaddle, who was standing with Tarko. Yoda raised his arm to silence the room and Master Sun rose from his chair, walking to the center of the room using a walking stick before beginning a funeral for Jedi Aida Forte, [Orin Darhga](/wiki/Orin_Darhga "Orin Darhga"), and Char-Ryl-Roy. Yoda allowed Roy's former Padawan, Keen, to keep his lightsaber and use it alongside hers.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

Later, in the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives"), Creighton spoke with Yoda about [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai") creatures that the Path deployed on Dalna and the horror they wrought upon the Jedi, causing them to be weakened, hallucinate, and eventually be turned to dust. Yoda confirmed that there is a larger danger connected to them, which caused Creighton to wonder what Yoda knew. Realizing how catastrophic to the Order it could be if people found out about the creatures, and since they had heard no other reports of their usage, they decided to keep quiet about them and not include them in the Jedi Archive. They agreed not to speak of it again and each of them left.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

#### Master of Kantam Sy

:   "*The lesson of Younglings we take on is one of the hardest ones for most Jedi to learn. Indeed, some never do."  
    "Detachment."  
    "To let go. Elusive it is, but also, always available to us, always there. And then, when we grasp, gone again. Takes practice, it does. Repetition. To have to do it again does not mean we have failed, only that we must do it again. And again.*"
:   ―Yoda and Kantam Sy[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

 [![Yoda held the title of Grand Master of the Jedi Order since the days of the High Republic Era.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/THRAdventures1Yoda-art.png/revision/latest?cb=20210204050207) [![Yoda held the title of Grand Master of the Jedi Order since the days of the High Republic Era.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/THRAdventures1Yoda-art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20210204050207)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/THRAdventures1Yoda-art.png/revision/latest?cb=20210204050207) 

Yoda held the title of Grand Master of the Jedi Order since the days of the High Republic Era.

 

At some point, Yoda took on a human named [Kantam Sy](/wiki/Kantam_Sy "Kantam Sy") as his Padawan. The two were stationed at the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Endovar) "Jedi Temple (Endovar)") on the planet [Endovar](/wiki/Endovar "Endovar"). Sy was a very talented Padawan and was far ahead of their peers and even some of their elders, with Yoda even admitting that they were the most disciplined Padawan he had ever taught and one of the most connected to the Force. Despite this, Yoda held off [knighting](/wiki/Knighting_Ceremony "Knighting Ceremony") Sy, for a reason that the Padawan did not understand until they began a romantic relationship with an [acrobat](/wiki/Acrobat "Acrobat") named [Aytar](/wiki/Aytar "Aytar") and realized that both Yoda and them had been waiting for something like that to happen. Eventually, Sy decided to leave the Jedi Order, a decision partially incited by their newfound relationship with Aytar.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

Yoda and Sy loved to spar with each other, and it was how the two often found understanding and how Sy often found inner harmony while troubled or when they had a problem. Even when they did not find a solution during a match, they would leave feeling like an answer was out there. When Sy traveled to the meditation room in the Endovar Jedi Temple in order to tell Yoda about their decision, Yoda challenged them to a sparring match, remembering that they had dueled many times in that room and saying that this duel could be one final lesson. Sy agreed to the duel, as it was custom to not refuse a duel with Master Yoda, but also realized that this meant Yoda knew about their decision. Yoda dodged Sy's question by engaging in combat, before saying that the time had come to make a choice, but not the one that Sy thought. Yoda explained that the Force chose Sy just as it had chosen all other Jedi, and asked when Sy would choose the Force. Sy insisted that they chose the Force every day when they took part in their Jedi training, but after knocking Sy to the ground, Yoda asked if we really make a choice when we do not believe there are any other options. Yoda told Sy that there was a reason he had not knighted them yet, before ending the duel, helping Sy up, and sitting down with Sy to meditate.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

Eventually Sy asked Yoda if they should leave the Jedi Order, but Yoda insisted that there was no 'should' and that the right thing to do is an idea we invent to make ourselves feel better. Yoda also suggested that Sy had stopped listening, in the literal sense, and in a larger general sense. Yoda explained that feelings are like wind, we can feel it, we can experience it, but it passes, though sometimes it can feel like a [hurricane](/wiki/Hurricane "Hurricane") which can make it easy to give in to anger and fear. Yoda told Sy that in order for them to continue to be a Jedi they must actively choose the Jedi Order and the Force and learn to listen to the world outside of their emotions even when they were as loud as a hurricane. Eventually, after a moment, Sy set down their lightsaber in front of Yoda. Yoda nodded at them, and then his Padawan left him, and the Jedi Order, behind. Yoda was saddened but supported Sy through their departure. Sy would reflect on the conversation they had that day throughout the rest of their life.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

Over a year later, Sy returned to the Jedi, and met with Yoda on the Endovar. Yoda was in the process of helping a pet [Happabore](/wiki/Happabore "Happabore") named [Monsalmo](/wiki/Monsalmo "Monsalmo") at the time, after being awoken from a nap by the creature's squealing. Yoda was used to dealing with her complicated behaviors, including finding her inside the temple underneath the younglings' bunks. This time, Monsalmo was pregnant and had climbed onto the roof of her pen to avoid giving birth in a [fuel](/wiki/Fuel "Fuel") spill. However, the roof could not hold the creature's weight and it collapsed. Yoda caught Monsalmo with the Force, but at that same time she started to give birth to her pups, so Yoda had to carry them with the Force too. Just then, Sy and a Force-sensitive girl they had rescued on the planet [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") named [Lula Talisola](/wiki/Lula_Mrala-Talisola "Lula Mrala-Talisola") arrived and both used the Force to help Yoda carry Monsalmo and her pups. Yoda welcomed Sy back, telling them that they had left a Padawan and returned a Knight. A few [hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour") later, Yoda knighted Sy in a modest ceremony so that they could take on Talisola as their Padawan learner.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

After the ceremony, Sy and Yoda sat around a fire near the happabore enclosure and discussed the events that had occurred. Sy expressed that they did not understand how one second they felt so sure in their path separate from the Order but was then pulled back to it when they saved Talisola. Yoda explained that the young are the greatest teachers and the greatest lesson that can be learned from them is necessity of detachment and letting go, that being a Jedi was to let go. Sy realized that they had been the one that taught Yoda that lesson. Yoda revealed that he had struggled with Sy's departure and had been unsure of the future. The two then shared [Sweetpuff jamwiches](/wiki/Sweetpuff_jamwich "Sweetpuff jamwich") with Talisola.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

 [![Yoda and Kantam Sy speak with Lula Talisola.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/LulaKantamYodaEndovarTemple-2021THRA12.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220607215930) [![Yoda and Kantam Sy speak with Lula Talisola.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/LulaKantamYodaEndovarTemple-2021THRA12.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20220607215930)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/LulaKantamYodaEndovarTemple-2021THRA12.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220607215930) 

Yoda and Kantam Sy speak with Lula Talisola.

 

Sometime later, Yoda and Sy met with Talisola in the Endovar Jedi temple. Sy told Talisola that the lesson she taught the two masters was the hardest one of all. Talisola hoped that it was front flips with a lightsaber, which made Sy retract their statement and say that it was the second hardest lesson to learn. Yoda concurred, saying that the front flip was nothing simple. But the lesson that Sy wanted to teach Talisola was the same one that Sy had learned from her and Yoda had learned from Sy: Detachment.[[34]](#cite_note-HRA_12-34)

Sometime before [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY"),[[35]](#cite_note-HRA_1_date-35) Yoda traveled to the [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Takodana) "Jedi Temple (Takodana)") on [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana") to pick up a Force-sensitive [Aloxian](/wiki/Aloxian "Aloxian") child named [Qort](/wiki/Qort "Qort") from [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata") and Jedi [Sav Malagán](/wiki/Savina_Besatrix_Malag%C3%A1n "Savina Besatrix Malagán") and bring him into the Jedi Order.[[36]](#cite_note-THRA_10-36) Padawan [Reath Silas](/wiki/Reath_Silas "Reath Silas") briefly met Yoda during some events both attended together.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

#### Time on the *Star Hopper*

:   "*Chaos on the surface, there will be. Remember that the Force moves through you, through* all *living things, even in chaos. Move with the Force, we must. Never against it.*"
:   ―Yoda during the [Trymant IV disaster](/wiki/Trymant_IV_disaster "Trymant IV disaster")[[37]](#cite_note-HRA_1-37)

By [233 BBY](/wiki/233_BBY "233 BBY"),[[38]](#cite_note-Date-38) Yoda was stationed alongside Master [Zia Zaldor Zanna](/wiki/Zia_Zaldor_Zanna "Zia Zaldor Zanna") at the Jedi Grand Temple on Coruscant assigning youngling Jedi Initiates to different [temple outposts](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") across the galaxy to continue learning and training under their teachers. Here he met initiates [Kai Brightstar](/wiki/Kai_Brightstar "Kai Brightstar"), [Lys Solay](/wiki/Lys_Solay "Lys Solay"), and [Nubs](/wiki/Nubs "Nubs"); Yoda gifted Brightstar his own [training saber](/wiki/Brightstar%27s_second_lightsaber "Brightstar's second lightsaber") after Brightstar sacrificed his to save Nubs while on a mission.[[39]](#cite_note-Meet_the_Young_Jedi-39) In 232 BBY,[[40]](#cite_note-THR_1_date-40) Yoda took a sabbatical from the Jedi Council,[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26) having felt the Force needed him on a different path. Thus, Yoda joined[[27]](#cite_note-THR_1-27) the crew of the Jedi [Padawan Academic Cruiser](/wiki/Padawan_Academic_Cruiser "Padawan Academic Cruiser") *[Star Hopper](/wiki/Star_Hopper "Star Hopper")*, allowing him to help [train](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") Padawans[[37]](#cite_note-HRA_1-37) and younglings.[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26) Yoda was also therefore able to help train Talisola, who was stationed aboard the *Star Hopper*.[[37]](#cite_note-HRA_1-37)

Yoda appointed the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") Jedi Master [Ephru Shinn](/wiki/Ephru_Shinn "Ephru Shinn") to hold his seat on the council while he was away. During the [Great Hyperspace Disaster](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Disaster "Great Hyperspace Disaster") in the [Hetzal system](/wiki/Hetzal_system "Hetzal system"), Jedi Master [Avar Kriss](/wiki/Avar_Kriss "Avar Kriss") established a Force [network](/wiki/Song_of_the_Force "Song of the Force"), which was eventually aided by Jedi who were outside the system. Yoda—located somewhere with the crew of younglings he was currently teaching—helped the effort, adding his focus to the network to ensure a [Tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna") [gas](/wiki/Gas "Gas") container did not collide with an [R-class](/wiki/R-class "R-class") [sun](/wiki/Star "Star").[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26)

 [![Yoda, Torban Buck, and Lula Talisola fight the Nihil on Trymant IV.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/TrymantIVAttack-2021THRA2.png/revision/latest?cb=20240211113817) [![Yoda, Torban Buck, and Lula Talisola fight the Nihil on Trymant IV.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/TrymantIVAttack-2021THRA2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240211113817)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/TrymantIVAttack-2021THRA2.png/revision/latest?cb=20240211113817) 

Yoda, Torban Buck, and Lula Talisola fight the Nihil on Trymant IV.

 

The Great [Hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") Disaster also caused the [Emergences](/wiki/Emergences "Emergences"), which were when giant pieces of debris exited hyperspace in various places throughout the galaxy and threatened to hit planets at near lightspeed. Eventually, the [Trymant system](/wiki/Trymant_system "Trymant system") was threatened by an [Emergence](/wiki/Trymant_IV_disaster "Trymant IV disaster"). The staff of [Republic Security Zone Monitoring Satellite 777B-Alpha](/wiki/Republic_Security_Zone_Monitoring_Satellite_777B-Alpha "Republic Security Zone Monitoring Satellite 777B-Alpha") reported the incident to the [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon") [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station"), who then asked the only Republic or Jedi ship immediately within range, the *Star Hopper*, to assist. Onboard was Yoda along with fellow Jedi Master [Torban Buck](/wiki/Torban_Buck "Torban Buck") and a class of Padawans. As they traveled through hyperspace to the Trymant system, Yoda told the Padawans to prepare for anything because they had no idea what was coming, but that the Force would reveal all. When they received the information that they were the only Republic or Jedi ship nearby to respond, one of the Padawans suggested that they stay back and wait for backup. But Yoda insisted that they were Trymant's only hope and needed to press forward. Shortly before they exited hyperspace Yoda had the Padawans report what information they had discovered about the calamity. Yoda and Buck decided to stay on the *Star Hopper* to use the Force to divert the biggest pieces of debris but sent the Padawans in [Rescue speeders](/wiki/Rescue_speeder "Rescue speeder") to help on the surface of the planet.[[37]](#cite_note-HRA_1-37)

However, amid the chaos of the Emergence, a [Spider Cruiser](/wiki/Spider_Cruiser "Spider Cruiser") called the *[Squall Spider](/wiki/Squall_Spider "Squall Spider")* commanded by the [Eye of the Nihil](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Nihil "Eye of the Nihil"), [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro") arrived in [Bralanak City](/wiki/Bralanak_City "Bralanak City") to pick up Elder Tromak, whom Ro wanted the services of to find some information. When the Padawans attempted to get [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") marauders to allow them to use the Spider Cruiser to evacuate civilians, a [fight](/wiki/Attack_on_Trymant_IV "Attack on Trymant IV") broke out,[[37]](#cite_note-HRA_1-37) leading Yoda and Buck to the surface to help the young Jedi and fight against the Nihil. During the fight, a Force-sensitive civilian named [Zeen Mrala](/wiki/Zeen_Mrala-Talisola "Zeen Mrala-Talisola") who had helped the Jedi against the Emergence and against the Nihil, told Masters Yoda and Buck that her friend [Krix Kamerat](/wiki/Krix_Kamerat "Krix Kamerat") had been captured by the Nihil and needed to be rescued. Lula Talisola offered to go, but Yoda insisted that he would go rescue the boy. Master Buck protested, believing that he was not a fighting Jedi and therefore should not be left to lead the Jedi, but Yoda ignored him. Yoda then protected the group of Jedi from a large plasma projectile lobbed at them by a Nihil marauder by cutting it into pieces with his lightsaber while it was still in the air. Yoda then left to find Kamerat, but first asked Mrala to take her pet [Cru](/wiki/Cru "Cru") [Cham Cham](/wiki/Cham_Cham "Cham Cham") with him.[[41]](#cite_note-HRA_2-41)

 [![Yoda discovers a piece of the Nameless control rod on a Nihil ship.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/PurpleGlow-2021THRA2.png/revision/latest?cb=20210304052322) [![Yoda discovers a piece of the Nameless control rod on a Nihil ship.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/PurpleGlow-2021THRA2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210304052322)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/PurpleGlow-2021THRA2.png/revision/latest?cb=20210304052322) 

Yoda discovers a piece of the Nameless control rod on a Nihil ship.

 

Marchion Ro knew of Yoda and his power, and when he saw him on the planet told his subordinates to keep the Jedi Master away from the *Squall Spider*, but Yoda managed to sneak aboard the ship nonetheless. Yoda eventually found Kamerat and told him that they needed to leave quickly. Yoda told Kamerat that Mrala had sent him and proved it by showing him Cham Cham. Yoda then gave Kamerat a [Holoprojector](/wiki/Holoprojector "Holoprojector") that he told the boy he could reach out to Mrala with when he was ready. However, Kamerat shortly after alerted the pirates that Yoda was aboard. Having been raised by the [Elders of the Path](/wiki/Elders_of_the_Path "Elders of the Path"),[[41]](#cite_note-HRA_2-41) a religious order descended from the Path of the Open Hand[[42]](#cite_note-CotJ-42) that distrusted Force-sensitives[[33]](#cite_note-HRA_5-33) due to believing the Force should only be appreciated from a distance, as if it was a fire,[[37]](#cite_note-HRA_1-37), only to see that his best friend Zeen Mrala had secretly been Force-sensitive and never told him, Kamerat felt betrayed and ended up siding with the Nihil because of that sense of betrayal. With the Nihil looking for him, Yoda ran from the marauders but uncovered that the Nihil had[[41]](#cite_note-HRA_2-41) a [strange, purple artifact](/wiki/Nameless_control_rods "Nameless control rods")[[33]](#cite_note-HRA_5-33) in a storage crate. Yoda hoped to escape quietly but Cham Cham made a loud cry that alerted the Nihil to their location and lead to a confrontation. Yoda escaped and met up with Mrala, revealing to her that Cham Cham had eaten several Nihil limbs in the confrontation. Yoda then told Mrala that she needed to come with them to Starlight Beacon. When she asked why he had not saved Kamerat, Yoda told her that he could not save someone who did not want to be rescued. With the Nihil drive from Trymant, Yoda, Torban Buck, Zeen Mrala, and the Padawans traveled to Starlight Beacon in the Star Hopper.[[41]](#cite_note-HRA_2-41)

#### Starlight Beacon

:   "*For light and life!*"  
    "*For light and life!*"
:   ―Yoda and the gathered Jedi, during the dedication of Starlight Beacon[[43]](#cite_note-YJA_Prince_and_the_Pirate-43)

Following the [Battle of Kur](/wiki/Battle_of_Kur "Battle of Kur"), Yoda went with fellow Grand Master Pra-Tre Veter to Starlight Beacon. The two had a meeting with the Supreme Chancellor [Lina Soh](/wiki/Lina_Soh "Lina Soh") to discuss [Bacta](/wiki/Bacta "Bacta") manufacturing for the relief effort for the Great Disaster, being in need of the right crops after what had occurred on [Hetzal](/wiki/Hetzal_Prime "Hetzal Prime"). But before their meeting, they visited the hub of the beacon to meet with Master Avar Kriss, and revealed to her that the council had convened and named her the [Marshal](/wiki/Marshal "Marshal") of Starlight Beacon. Kriss also asked Yoda if he was returning to the council, but Yoda clarified that he was not finished on the *Star Hopper*.[[27]](#cite_note-THR_1-27) Yoda later attended the Beacon's [dedication ceremony](/wiki/Dedication_of_the_Starlight_Beacon "Dedication of the Starlight Beacon"), where he said a few words about the [dedication plaque](/wiki/Dedication_plaque "Dedication plaque") which was placed in a stone monument. He talked with Kai Brightstar, Lys Solay, [Nash Durango](/wiki/Nash_Durango "Nash Durango"), and Nubs, mentioning their adventure trying to get the dedication plaque after it was stolen by the pirate [Taborr Val Dorn](/wiki/Cyrus_Vuundir "Cyrus Vuundir"), who was secretly Prince Cyrus Vuundir of [Vuundalla](/wiki/Vuundalla "Vuundalla"). He told them how proud he is of them and encouraged them to join the rest of the Jedi for Lina Soh's speech. After the Jedi left, Yoda spoke with Prince Vuundir, who was no longer in his pirate disguise, telling him that he sensed much conflict in him but that he still had the potential for greatness if he made the right choices. Yoda told Cyrus that the future was in his hands. Joining with his fellow Jedi, he raised his [lightsaber](/wiki/Yoda%27s_lightsaber "Yoda's lightsaber") and declared "For light and life."[[43]](#cite_note-YJA_Prince_and_the_Pirate-43)

 [![Yoda discusses Zeen Mrala and the Nihil's secrets with Estala Maru and Avar Kriss.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/MaruYodaKrissDiscussion-2021THRA3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210408091341) [![Yoda discusses Zeen Mrala and the Nihil's secrets with Estala Maru and Avar Kriss.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/MaruYodaKrissDiscussion-2021THRA3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20210408091341)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/MaruYodaKrissDiscussion-2021THRA3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210408091341) 

Yoda discusses Zeen Mrala and the Nihil's secrets with Estala Maru and Avar Kriss.

 

After about a week, Zeen Mrala started settling in on Starlight very well, so Masters Yoda, Avar Kriss, Kantam Sy, [Estala Maru](/wiki/Estala_Maru "Estala Maru"), and Torban Buck all went to check up on her and discuss her plans, with Yoda even bringing pastry treats. The Masters deliberated and determined that she was too old to begin Jedi training and most likely could not be sent back to Trymant. Master Sy suggested that she should stay with them temporarily, as she had proved herself valuable, which Yoda acknowledged was an excellent point. They did decide to let her stay, partially with the hope that she could be helpful against the Nihil. When it became clear that finding the Nihil would be a challenge, Yoda revealed that he had given a holoprojector to Kamerat and one to Mrala. Mrala confirmed that they had had communications, which she apologized for, but Yoda denied her apology and said that she might have just saved the day. Yoda explained that they could use the holoprojectors to track the Nihil, but would have to be relatively close. Yoda was determined to find the Nihil to figure out what the mysterious artifact he had found was. The Jedi decided to travel to the [Bright Jewel system](/wiki/Bright_Jewel_system "Bright Jewel system"), as there had been recent Nihil activity there, and see if they could pick up a signal.[[44]](#cite_note-HRA_3-44)

 [![Yoda flies a Jedi Vector in the Battle in the Bright Jewel system.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/YodaVector-2021THRA4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220608032838) [![Yoda flies a Jedi Vector in the Battle in the Bright Jewel system.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/YodaVector-2021THRA4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20220608032838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/YodaVector-2021THRA4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220608032838) 

Yoda flies a Jedi Vector in the Battle in the Bright Jewel system.

 

In the Bright Jewel system, a routine got into a skirmish with a group of Nihil raiders, who alerted the [Republic Outpost](/wiki/Republic_Outpost "Republic Outpost") on [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell"). Yoda, Torban Buck, Kantam Sy, and many other Jedi flew [Jedi Vectors](/wiki/Jedi_Vector "Jedi Vector") out of the outpost to confront the Nihil. The conflict erupted into an all out [battle](/wiki/Battle_in_the_Bright_Jewel_system "Battle in the Bright Jewel system"). Eventually all of the Nihil fighters were defeated, but Yoda was concerned, as he thought that it was too easy and that there therefore might be something wrong. Then the Jedi received a distress signal that they first believed was from the Ord Mantell base, until Yoda suspected that it was not actually from the base. They determined the signal to be from the junk [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") [Quantxi](/wiki/Quantxi "Quantxi"), and so Yoda ordered the Jedi to travel to the moon and send for backup from Starlight Beacon, though he also worried that they were too late.[[45]](#cite_note-HRA_4-45)

#### Disappearance

:   "*Master Yoda is still missing. As you all know, he was my Master when I was a Padawan and I wish he were here too. But he told us not to follow him and we must trust the Force on this.*"
:   ―Kantam Sy[[13]](#cite_note-HRA_8-13)

 [![Yoda and Elder Tromak's shuttle is shot down over Vrant Tarnum.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/VrantTarnum-2021THRA5.png/revision/latest?cb=20210707000509) [![Yoda and Elder Tromak's shuttle is shot down over Vrant Tarnum.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/VrantTarnum-2021THRA5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210707000509)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/VrantTarnum-2021THRA5.png/revision/latest?cb=20210707000509) 

Yoda and Elder Tromak's shuttle is shot down over Vrant Tarnum.

 

Yoda journeyed to the junk moon of Quantxi with Masters Torban Buck and Kantam Sy to aid the Padawans of the *Star Hopper* against the Nihil force stationed there. However, Yoda crossed paths with Elder Tromak, who had escaped the Nihil after being escorted off Trymant IV with Kamerat by Ro, after landing. Yoda recognized him from Trymant. Tromak offered the Jedi [bogaranths](/wiki/Bogaranth "Bogaranth") to ride to the Nihil, clarifying that even though he hated Jedi, they had a common enemy. As Masters Sy and Buck saddled up onto the bogaranths, Tromak pulled Yoda aside. Reminding Yoda of their meeting on Dalna years prior, he asked the Grand Master to journey with him to [Kharvashark Ruins](/wiki/Kharvashark_Ruins "Kharvashark Ruins") on [Vrant Tarnum](/wiki/Vrant_Tarnum "Vrant Tarnum") to stop the Nihil from recovering the second half of the mysterious artifact, with Yoda informing Tromak that the Nihil already had half of the weapon. However, Tromak was inistent on keeping the artifact's location a secret, so he told Yoda that he could not bring his comlink. Yoda agreed to this, and after sending one last message to the other Jedi telling them not to follow him, the two traveled to the [Stygmarn system](/wiki/Stygmarn_system "Stygmarn system") above Vrant Tarnum. However, the two encountered a network of drones and were shot down, allowing Ro a to acquire the other half of the artifact.[[33]](#cite_note-HRA_5-33)

To the Jedi Order at large, Yoda was suddenly missing in action.[[46]](#cite_note-RtCT-46) As the [Drengir crisis](/wiki/Drengir_crisis "Drengir crisis") and [conflict](/wiki/Nihil_conflict "Nihil conflict") with the Nihil dragged on, Yoda's name became one of the many mentioned alongside Jedi who had gone missing or died during the conflicts.[[47]](#cite_note-HRA_7-47) He was still missing by the time of the [attack on Valo](/wiki/Valo_Atrocity "Valo Atrocity")[[46]](#cite_note-RtCT-46) and ensuing [Battle of Grizal](/wiki/Battle_of_Grizal "Battle of Grizal"),[[13]](#cite_note-HRA_8-13) which both marked major escalations in tensions in the struggle between the Republic and the Nihil. In the latter engagement, Ro unleashed the living weapon known as the [Great Leveler](/wiki/Great_Leveler "Great Leveler") against the Jedi for the first time, using the completed artifact to control it.[[48]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-48) Remembering that Yoda told them and Buck not to follow him, Sy told the *Star Hopper*'s Padawans, after they asked whether they could go searching for the missing Jedi Master, that they needed to trust in the Force.[[13]](#cite_note-HRA_8-13) But Yoda's departure affected the *Star Hopper*'s close crew in an incredibly deep way.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

 [![Amid the stress of the Nihil conflict, the Jedi of Starlight Beacon use one of Yoda's recipes to come together and better understand each other.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/StarlightBakingDay-THRABakeOff.png/revision/latest?cb=20240211113451) [![Amid the stress of the Nihil conflict, the Jedi of Starlight Beacon use one of Yoda's recipes to come together and better understand each other.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/StarlightBakingDay-THRABakeOff.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/215?cb=20240211113451)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/StarlightBakingDay-THRABakeOff.png/revision/latest?cb=20240211113451) 

Amid the stress of the Nihil conflict, the Jedi of Starlight Beacon use one of Yoda's recipes to come together and better understand each other.

 

During the [skirmish on Xais](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Xais "Skirmish on Xais"), Master Avar Kriss recalled Yoda's wisdom when Master [Sskeer](/wiki/Sskeer "Sskeer") started to utilize extreme violence again, remembering him frequently saying that once you walk to the dark path it's forever in your heart.[[49]](#cite_note-THR_11-49) Sometime later, Masters Kantam Sy and Torban Buck gathered a group of Jedi to bake Master Yoda's recipe for special baked sweet story custard cakes. The Masters claimed that the recipe specifically stated that the only way for the [cakes](/wiki/Cake "Cake") to come out correctly is if the bakers told a story about cooperation while baking them, one in which they expanded their knowledge of what they were capable of, found trust in another person, or found a deeper understanding of the Force.[[50]](#cite_note-Bake_Off-50)

Later, when Sy was assigned to investigate Nihil activity on [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia") with Master [Cohmac Vitus](/wiki/Cohmac_Vitus "Cohmac Vitus"), Sy mentioned that the young were the greatest teachers they could have, besides Master Yoda. This prompted Vitus to ask if there was any word on the old Jedi Master, to which Sy explained that they could not feel him, but that it did not necessarily mean anything. Sy expressed their belief that if Yoda had died, they all would have felt it, but Cohmac was still concerned with how long he had been gone despite that. Sy also lamented that it felt like everything happening would be much easier to make sense of if Yoda were there. Later, at Vitus's asking, Sy revealed to him that Master Yoda had let them do a walkabout of the Jedi Order, as he knew if he did not it would have been the end of things between Sy and the Order, with Sy even telling Vitus the entire story including Yoda's influence during the day they left and the day they returned to the Order. Cohmac also told Sy that they wondered what Yoda would make of everything that was happening.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

After the [Battle at Dol'har Hyde](/wiki/Battle_at_Dol%27har_Hyde "Battle at Dol'har Hyde"), an engagement that saw the capture of Nihil leader Krix Kamerat and his detainment aboard the *Star Hopper*, Zeen Mrala and Lula Talisola visited Yoda's old quarters on the ship and reflected on the Jedi Master. Mrala missed him in a way that she thought was only possible to miss someone you had known your whole life, and especially missed the Jedi's welcoming presence and his laughing face. She thought that they needed Yoda's help more than ever since they had captured Kamerat. Mrala asked Talisola if she thought Yoda was ever coming back, and Talisola declared that he definitely was and that he would not want them to be standing there worrying about him.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

Padawans Reath Silas and [Ram Jomaram](/wiki/Ram_Jomaram "Ram Jomaram") also reflected on Yoda's disappearance while on Corellia, with Silas saying that he seemed like he would have been a "pretty fun" Master to Kantam Sy and that he remembered being able to feel Yoda's wisdom from a mile away. Both were Padawans were plagued with anxiety over Yoda's disappearance and imagined nightmare scenarios about what happened to him, which they admitted to each other. Silas mused that if Yoda were there, he would have said "Forgive himself, a Jedi must, mm? Not being ruled by fear does not mean not feeling any fear at all, mm!" which Jomaram thought sounded very accurate.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

#### Return

:   "*To do this, though, to forge our path to the future, guided by the secrets of the past, we will be.*"
:   ―Yoda[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

Concurrent to the [destruction of Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon"), Sy, Vitus, Jomaram, Silas, and Mrala joined Corellian bodyguards and civilians in [fighting Nihil](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Corellian_Shipyards "Battle of the Corellian Shipyards") who were attempting to steal a fleet of [MPO-1400 Purgill-class star cruisers](/wiki/MPO-1400_Purgill-class_star_cruiser "MPO-1400 Purgill-class star cruiser") and Republic [Longbeam cruisers](/wiki/Longbeam-class_corvette "Longbeam-class corvette") from the [shipyards](/wiki/Santhe_Shipyards "Santhe Shipyards") in [Coronet City](/wiki/Coronet_City "Coronet City") on Corellia in order to add to the chaos and destruction of the space station. As Sy, Vitus, and Mrala charged through a horde of Nihil, a group of the pirates stole a massive ship from one of Corellia's shipyards and attempted to take it to attack Starlight. However, the three Force-sensitives used the Force to stall the trawler and prevent it from escaping, but they had a weak hold on it and as they did Nihil reinforcements arrived. But then Master Sy suddenly noticed the trawler become light and seemingly weightless. And then the remaining Nihil [war cloud](/wiki/War_cloud "War cloud") was swept away suddenly, confusing the pirates, but also revealing Master Yoda in hooded robes holding the trawler with the Force with his lightsaber ignited at his side.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

Yoda told Sy that it seemed like they needed a hand, and Sy collapsed and started cry at the sight of their old Master. Yoda then used the Force to send the massive ship crashing onto the horde of Nihil reinforcements with a fiery explosion. When more Nihil came, Yoda threw himself into their leader feet first and then used the Force to knock the others down with a single hand motion. This inspired Sy, who shouted "For light and life" before joining up with Vitus and Mrala again and fighting by Yoda's side. Yoda and Sy worked together to take down a Nihil with a [buzz saw](/wiki/Circular_saw "Circular saw"), Sy knocking him off balance before Yoda stabbed him in the back with his lightsaber. The Jedi then regrouped with the [Corellian](/wiki/Corellian "Corellian") fighters and Yoda shouted the rallying cry "For light and life" which spread throughout the crowd. Eventually they managed to drive the Nihil away, winning the battle.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

 [![The Nameless (pictured) emerged as a massive threat to the Jedi Order, but Yoda's quest for answers brought him to Azlin Rell who had had a connection to the beings.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/NamelessStarlightBeacon-THRTrailOfShadows5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220210014635) [![The Nameless (pictured) emerged as a massive threat to the Jedi Order, but Yoda's quest for answers brought him to Azlin Rell who had had a connection to the beings.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/NamelessStarlightBeacon-THRTrailOfShadows5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220210014635)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/NamelessStarlightBeacon-THRTrailOfShadows5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220210014635) 

The Nameless (pictured) emerged as a massive threat to the Jedi Order, but Yoda's quest for answers brought him to Azlin Rell who had had a connection to the beings.

 

Afterward, Jomaram, who had been instrumental to the Jedi's success elsewhere in the battle, reunited with Sy, who introduced him to Yoda. Yoda said that they had much to discuss and not enough time, to which Sy added that they needed a place to go where they could regroup safely and debrief. [Alys "Crash" Ongwa](/wiki/Alys_Ongwa "Alys Ongwa"), one of the leaders of the Corellian fighters offered up a location to the Jedi. The group, including Yoda, ended up taking refuge in the hideaway of [Baynoo Ongwa](/wiki/Baynoo_Ongwa "Baynoo Ongwa"), Crash Ongwa's mother, in [The Green](/wiki/The_Green "The Green") on Corellia, riding various ships and airspeeders to get there. There, they were joined by a mysterious hooded individual,[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25) the former Jedi Knight [Azlin Rell](/wiki/Azlin_Rell "Azlin Rell"),[[51]](#cite_note-Shadows_of_Starlight_1-51) who had accompanied Yoda. Rell did not sho his face or speak to anyone, and only constantly quietly sang the nursery rhyme '[Shrii ka rai ka rai](/wiki/Shrii_ka_rai_ka_rai "Shrii ka rai ka rai")',[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25) which had a connection to the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai"),[[52]](#cite_note-Trail_of_Shadows_5-52) over and over again. Yoda declared that there was much to explain without actually explaining anything, but nobody questioned him under the assumption that there would be time to do so later. The group ate, bathed, and then tried to sleep.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

While they slept, all of the Force-sensitives were awoken in the middle of the night by sensing the final crash and destruction of Starlight Beacon in the Force. After feeling the death of Jedi [Orla Jareni](/wiki/Orla_Jareni "Orla Jareni") aboard Starlight Beacon, Master Cohmac Vitus gathered Yoda, the other Jedi, Zeen Mrala, and his Padawan Reath Silas. Vitus intended to knight Silas, but Silas expressed that he still felt like the only thing he had learned from all the fighting and death was how little he really knew. But Yoda commended this, saying that it was perhaps one of the hardest and most important lessons to learn. Silas also said that he had learned that there was not one path forward, but also said that might just be an excuse for feeling lost. Yoda assured him that it was impossible to be lost when there was not one right way forward. After more questions from Silas, Yoda then asked jokingly if he thought all of those Masters that thought he was ready were wrong. This prompted Silas to say he was ready, and together Masters Yoda, Vitus, and Sy knighted Reath Silas. But Master Vitus then handed his lightsaber to Silas, and after exchanging nods with Yoda, left the house, and left the Jedi Order for good.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

The next morning, Yoda and Sy chatted and readied to leave, while Zeen Mrala reflected on the moment that Yoda had joined the battle with joy and inspiration. Yoda walked up to Crash Ongwa and [Deemus Abrus](/wiki/Deemus_Abrus "Deemus Abrus"), who had helped the Jedi before the battle, and wished them farewell. Yoda told the two that a new threat had arisen and that all of the Jedi needed to return to Jedi Temple on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), prompting Sy to reveal that the [recall signal](/wiki/Jedi_beacon "Jedi beacon") that Yoda had asked for had been sent out minutes earlier. Yoda explained that the way forward would be difficult, but that they would manage to find a way by being guided by the secrets of the past.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25) Part of this involved Rell, whose years of research on the Nameless Yoda hoped could help them learn how to fight or stop the beasts.[[51]](#cite_note-Shadows_of_Starlight_1-51)

#### Speaking with Rwoh

:   "*Sorry to disturb you, Master. We need to talk.*"
:   ―Vernestra Rwoh to Yoda[[53]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte_(episode)-53)

In [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY"), Jedi Master [Vernestra Rwoh](/wiki/Vernestra_Rwoh "Vernestra Rwoh") approached Yoda to speak with him after she had interrogated a memory-wiped [Mae-ho Aniseya](/wiki/Mae-ho_Aniseya "Mae-ho Aniseya"), who had not even known about the existence of her sister, former Jedi [Verosha Aniseya](/wiki/Verosha_Aniseya "Verosha Aniseya"). The Jedi Grandmaster was seated with his face towards her when he was approached. Afterwards,[[53]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte_(episode)-53) Yoda became involved in the Osha-Mae situation, which proved to be a stressful time for the Jedi Master.[[54]](#cite_note-WinLose-54)

### Master of Dooku

:   "*Perhaps the best Padawan of your generation, you were.*"  
    "*Are you resorting to* flattery*, Master Yoda? Besides, I recall getting into more* trouble *than any other Padawan of my generation.*"  
    "*Yes. And a* valuable *perspective, this gives you.*"
:   ―Yoda and Dooku reflect on their time together as master and apprentice[[55]](#cite_note-Yoda_4-55)

 [![Yoda was the Jedi Master of Count Dooku, who ultimately renounced his commitment to the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/YodaDookuDuelingDemo-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190215020827) [![Yoda was the Jedi Master of Count Dooku, who ultimately renounced his commitment to the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/YodaDookuDuelingDemo-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190215020827)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/YodaDookuDuelingDemo-AORDooku1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190215020827) 

Yoda was the Jedi Master of Count Dooku, who ultimately renounced his commitment to the Jedi Order.

 

Several decades later,[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Yoda took on the human [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") as his last known Padawan in the era of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic").[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) In [90 BBY](/wiki/90_BBY "90 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Yoda undertook a visit to Serenno with other Jedi Masters and younglings Sifo Dyas, and Dooku. Yoda later took Dooku on as an apprentice in[[56]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-56) [86 BBY](/wiki/86_BBY "86 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) and while Dooku initially wanted to become the Padawan of [Lene Kostana](/wiki/Lene_Kostana "Lene Kostana"), his disappointment subsided when he learned he would be Yoda's apprentice. Once on a visit to Serenno, Master and apprentice together, Dooku's father shouted at the Grand Master for bringing his son to the planet, holding a dislike for the Jedi Order and Force-sensitives.[[56]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-56) During one mission to the [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), Dooku witnessed his master face off with a giant, dreadful [terentatek](/wiki/Terentatek "Terentatek").[[57]](#cite_note-Destiny-57) Decades after his apprentice graduated to Knighthood,[[56]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-56) in [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Yoda was informed by Dooku that he was departing from the Jedi Order, much to his disappointment, and when his former student offered to turn over his lightsaber, the Grandmaster allowed him to retain ownership of his weapon.[[56]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-56)

### Yoda's secret war

#### Answering a call

:   "*Not on their own are your children. But wrestling with the chaos you left them in. Blame them I do not. Better teachers they deserved.*"
:   ―Master Yoda, to the missing parents of Vagadarr Prime[[58]](#cite_note-SW_28-58)

Around 40 BBY,[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Yoda rescued a Force-sensitive child named [Lo](/wiki/Lo "Lo") from the [Flesh Mongers](/wiki/Flesh_Mongers "Flesh Mongers") on the planet [Botor](/wiki/Botor "Botor"), intending to begin his Jedi training. After dealing with the pirates, the Jedi Master was joined by Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") and his Padawan, [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), who had been tasked with escorting the child to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant. While on Botor, Yoda sensed a disturbance in the Force and chose to follow its call which led him to [Vagadarr Prime](/wiki/Vagadarr_Prime "Vagadarr Prime"). Upon landing on the planet's surface, the Jedi Master was suddenly surrounded by child warriors who attacked him. After defending himself with the Force, Yoda told the children he meant no harm. The Jedi came in peace as he was drawn in by the Force. The group realized he had heard their [Skyscream](/wiki/Skyscream "Skyscream"), and believed his [Stonepower](/wiki/Stonepower "Stonepower") to be strong. They then led Yoda to their home, [Mucktown](/wiki/Mucktown "Mucktown"). There, he learned that the [Skyscreamers](/wiki/Skyscreamers "Skyscreamers") used shards of the [Sacred rock](/wiki/Sacred_rock "Sacred rock") during their prayer, the same call that Yoda felt. The rock was unlike anything he had ever seen before. It was a piece of [blue stone](/wiki/Blue_stone "Blue stone"), a type of rock imbued with the Living Force which Yoda could sense. The [Mud dwellers](/wiki/Mud_dwellers "Mud dwellers") told him about their war against the [Rockhawkers](/wiki/Rockhawkers "Rockhawkers"), a rival tribe. He listened to the history of their homeworld, and how the conflict began. Long ago, people lived in harmony near the [Blue mountains](/wiki/Blue_mountains "Blue mountains"), but some craved the power of the stones. This greed divided them into warring factions and ultimately destroyed most of the mountains. Only one remained, known as the [Great Mountain](/wiki/Great_Mountain "Great Mountain"), which was claimed by the Rockhawkers who then banished the Mud dwellers to the [Mud Fields](/wiki/Mud_Fields "Mud Fields"). They carried as much stone as they could for their children, now the only survivors of the tribe. The children then led Yoda to a [boy](/wiki/Unidentified_Mud_dweller_prisoner "Unidentified Mud dweller prisoner") from the rival tribe they had taken prisoner. The Jedi sensed his deep fear of the Great Mountain, the sacred home of his tribe. As the children argued over his fate, Yoda urged them not to be consumed by fear. He asked them to release the child so that he could guide the Jedi to his people.[[59]](#cite_note-SW_26-59)[[60]](#cite_note-SW_27-60)

#### Exploring the Mountain

After walking to the Mountain, Yoda and the freed boy reached the Rockhawkers who attacked him with the stones. Refusing to fight back, the Jedi Master was captured. The tribe then sent him on a mission to find the [Heart of the Mountain](/wiki/Heart_of_the_Mountain "Heart of the Mountain"), accompanied by the boy he just saved. Yoda began to climb the path leading to the Heart, but his companion was overcome by fear, convinced that only death awaited them, just like all those who had climbed before. Despite Yoda's efforts to reassure him, the boy fell to his death. At the end of the path, the Jedi entered a [cave](/wiki/Old_Ones%27_caves "Old Ones' caves") where he encountered the lost parents, known as the [Old Ones](/wiki/Old_Ones_(Vagadarr_system) "Old Ones (Vagadarr system)"), who had once been sent by their children to find the Heart of the Mountain. They marked their parents with the symbol of the [Ancient Ones](/wiki/Ancient_Ones "Ancient Ones"), their long-gone ancestors. The Old Ones told Yoda they chose not to leave this place, preferring the peace they found within the mountain to the war raging outside. Yoda replied that they abandoned their children to the very war they had provoked. He continued exploring the cave and came across a child named [Garro](/wiki/Garro "Garro"), abandoned by the Rockhawkers, who believed he was too weak. After saving him, Yoda asked the boy to become his teacher and show him the ways of the Stonepower. During their training, the Jedi Master discovered the Heart of the Mountain and realized that the stone was not only alive in the Force but was in fact a living being. After nine days of communion, Yoda heard its voice. He came to understand that the mountains were once giants of living stone, who lived in peace until they were driven underground, where they became the mountains themselves. Yoda and Garro eventually emerged from the cave. But the Jedi chose not to reveal what he had learned to the Rockhawkers. Enraged, the tribe threatened him. However, Garro revealed the secret of the mountains to his people, brought Yoda’s teaching to an end, and returned to his faction.[[60]](#cite_note-SW_27-60)[[58]](#cite_note-SW_28-58)[[61]](#cite_note-SW_29-61)

#### Last battle

Yoda returned to the Mud Dwellers to warn them of an inevitable war. Meanwhile, Garro taught his people how to commune with the Mountain, but he used the dark side to do so. Yoda encouraged the Mud Dwellers to pray and help awaken the stones. Soon, the Rockhawkers caused the Mountain to rise from the ground, but Yoda decided to face it alone. Drawing strength from the Force, the Jedi resisted the Mountain’s fury, which had been fueled by revenge. Shortly after, other beings of living stone awoke and joined Yoda in his struggle. Together, they defeated the Mountain. As Garro and his warriors charged at the Jedi Master, Yoda pleaded with the boy to find peace within himself and with the stones, so the war could end. Garro dropped his weapon and abandoned the fight. The war was over. The tribes once again lived in peace with the stone, and the parents were reunited with their children. Many left the planet after hearing Yoda speak of the other worlds in the galaxy. Upon leaving, Yoda kept the secret of the Mountain to himself, sharing only the lesson he had learned with Obi-Wan Kenobi: "A Jedi must humble himself before he can ever be powerful."[[61]](#cite_note-SW_29-61)[[12]](#cite_note-SW_30-12)

### Pre-Invasion of Naboo

Yoda visited Kashyyyk on several other occasions prior to the [Battle of Kashyyyk](/wiki/Battle_of_Kashyyyk "Battle of Kashyyyk"), serving as Jedi negotiator in many incidents involving the Wookiees and their [Trandoshan](/wiki/Trandoshan "Trandoshan") neighbors. This earned him the ancient title of "[Defender of the Home Tree](/wiki/Defender_of_the_Home_Tree "Defender of the Home Tree")," as well as becoming a member of many Wookiee leaders' and all the inhabitants of [Kachirho](/wiki/Kachirho "Kachirho")'s honor families.[[62]](#cite_note-CL-62)

Yoda also taught outside the Master/Padawan relationship, and trained all the Jedi younglings prior to their teaming up with Jedi Masters,[[63]](#cite_note-SWE-Yoda-63) including Master [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi").[[64]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_Kenobi-64) Since his days as a youngling, [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), a human who would eventually rise to become part of the Jedi Council, never responded well to the Grand Master's humor, which became one of the reasons Yoda continued to use his humor.[[65]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-65) [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"), as Caleb Dume, often heard Yoda counsel, "Do, or do not.
