A probe droid then appeared and Yoda quickly took out a pot given to him by Kenobi. He used the Force to smash it into the droid only to suddenly sense Kenobi's death at the hands of Darth Vader. With the Jedi distracted, two more droids arrived but Yoda crushed them both and continued on home.[[106]](#cite_note-FACPOV-106)

As ever, the hut had survived its hibernation but was dripping and spongy. Five days later, Yoda had dried and cleaned the house. Each time he saw the shelf usually reserved for his pot, he reacted with some loneliness after destroying Obi-Wan's gift to him. Feeling his isolation, he reached out to the netherworld of the Force to speak to Qui-Gon Jinn, but the spirit of Obi-Wan answered instead and requested that Skywalker's child be trained. Having harbored regrets about not having taken the man's daughter as his apprentice, and assuaged that he had enough time left to teach another pupil, the Jedi Master readily agreed until he found out that Kenobi was actually speaking of Anakin's unfocused son instead. Nevertheless, Yoda begrudgingly allowed Kenobi to direct the boy to him.[[106]](#cite_note-FACPOV-106) As Yoda ruminated on his decision afterwards, he returned to the "Cave of Evil" and was reassured that the site had no new fears to show him.[[104]](#cite_note-FACPOV2-104)

#### A phantom visitor

:   "*Yoda had to know all of that. He could have killed me or let the planet do it for him. Instead…he chose to teach me.*"
:   ―The Archivist[[114]](#cite_note-CR_3-114)

Sometime later, a mysterious woman once known as Madelin Sun who became known as "[The Archivist](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist")" arrived on Dagobah in search of Yoda at the behest of Lady [Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra"), the leader of the crime syndicate [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"), who wanted Yoda's help to take down the Sith. When the Archivist was attacked by a monster after arriving on the planet, Yoda used the Force to save her from a distance and then led her into the dark side cave in order to dissuade her from looking for him. Having a change of heart, she left the planet as Yoda watched from afar. The Archivist returned to Qi'ra, lying and telling her that Yoda was dead.[[114]](#cite_note-CR_3-114)

#### Haunted by Kenobi

:   "*The shadow that has fallen across the galaxy…my fault, it is. I have exiled myself here, not just for penance. I have removed myself from events…because without me, better off the galaxy is.*"
:   ―Yoda to the spirit of Kenobi[[115]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_9-115)

Three years after agreeing to train Skywalker,[[116]](#cite_note-Comic_date-116) Kenobi contacted Yoda, who at first ignored the late Jedi Master's spirit. Kenobi urged Yoda to see reason and acknowledge the growing darkness in the galaxy. Yoda mused that the threat had become too powerful—too big—for him to defeat, to which Kenobi reminded Yoda of the first lesson the latter would teach new Jedi: "size matters not." Yoda admitted that he had sensed Kenobi's demise and had been avoiding him on purpose, once again expressing a defeatist attitude to the situation at hand. Kenobi dismissed the notion, not believing it himself and saying he did not think Yoda believed it either. Yoda reflected on his own inability to stop Darth Sidious and the fall of Anakin Skywalker, stating the galaxy was better off without him.[[115]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_9-115)

Yoda later had a dream in which [Bree Menaren](/wiki/Bree_Menaren "Bree Menaren"), Yoda's old pupil, taught and encouraged him to play the [taratti](/wiki/Taratti "Taratti"). Yoda, sensing something was amiss, turned to see the sky blocked out by a massive battle station. The Jedi Master drew his lightsaber to find himself facing an apparation of Anakin Skywalker as a Padawan, his eyes glowing yellow, also encouraging Yoda to play with the toy. Activating his weapon, Yoda was confronted with a twisted vision of an undead Qui-Gon Jinn, who berated Yoda for his ignorance before engaging him in a brief lightsaber duel. Yoda began to deny his claims, only to be annihilated by a blinding green light crashing down from the superweapon above.[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

Yoda woke from the nightmare to find Kenobi at his side. When Yoda questioned the spirit's continued presence, Kenobi stated that he would remain until Yoda agreed to hear him out and do as he asked. The elder Jedi master, looking to get away from Kenobi, set out from his hut to find herbs for his soup. Kenobi followed, reminiscing about times past and reminding Yoda about his making pastries when Kenobi was but a youngling. Not finding any herbs, Yoda remarked he had made a wrong turn only to realize that he and Kenobi had arrived at the Cave of Evil—exactly where Yoda needed to be, Kenobi opined, "from a certain point of view."[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

#### Entering the Cave of Evil

:   "*But what of you, old friend? Will you be ready when he comes?*"  
    "*Ready to teach? Yes, I will. Ready to teach—and ready to learn.*"
:   ―The spirit of Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda, after the latter went in the Cave of Evil[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

Yoda refused to go inside, believing that was what Kenobi wanted of him, to which Kenobi merely asked Yoda if he thought that would be the right course of action. Yoda noted that the location was stong in the dark side and had nothing to prove, with Kenobi reasoning that his fellow master should therefore have nothing to fear. Yoda dismissed the venture as a foolish waste of time but relented nonetheless.[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

Entering the vergence, Yoda was startled by a creature of Dagobah's wildlife, the Jedi Master grumbling that he had become old and foolish. Yoda was then confronted by a voice from the shadows—an apparation of Dooku, his former apprentice. The illusion blamed Yoda for his fall to the Dark Side, revealing his hand in the death of Yaddle and beginning to duel Yoda. Yoda then experienced a vision of High Republic Era Jedi [Keeve Trennis](/wiki/Keeve_Trennis "Keeve Trennis"), who refused to help Yoda and, like Dooku, blamed him for her final fate.[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

 [![Yoda has a vision of Keeve Trennis in the Cave of Evil while fighting an apparition of Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/TrennisYodaDooku-Yoda10.png/revision/latest?cb=20240607113256) [![Yoda has a vision of Keeve Trennis in the Cave of Evil while fighting an apparition of Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/TrennisYodaDooku-Yoda10.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240607113256)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/TrennisYodaDooku-Yoda10.png/revision/latest?cb=20240607113256) 

Yoda has a vision of Keeve Trennis in the Cave of Evil while fighting an apparition of Dooku.

 

Trennis used the Force to push Yoda into a mound of skulls, which a burning Anakin Skywalker claimed to be the Jedi Master's failures—those who had died. Bail Organa, Padmé Amidala, and Mace Windu emerged from the grave, reminding Yoda that they had looked to him for answers. Yoda replied that he could not have known how things would ultimately turn out, only for a spectre of Darth Sidious to cite the Jedi Master as the greatest of his apprentices, blind and unaware. Sidious noted there way no way back because of him, to which Yoda began repeating the phrase and drowning in the pile of corpses.[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

It was then that Bree appeared, reminding the Jedi Master that there was no situation was entirely without hope—something he had learned from Yoda himself. Bree elaborated that one could make as many mistakes as was required because, as Yoda finished the thought for him, "the greatest teacher, failure is." Yoda remembered the lessons of the Jedi and struck down the remaining ghosts of his past.[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

Exiting the cave, Yoda found Kenobi waiting for him. Yoda answered an affirmative to the question on Kenobi's mind, agreeing to train the son of Anakin Skywalker. Removing Bree's taratti from his robe, Yoda stated that he was ready to teach but also ready to learn.[[117]](#cite_note-Yoda_comic_10-117)

#### Taking a new apprentice

:   "*Do, or do not. There is no try.*"
:   ―Yoda to Luke Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/ThereIsNoTry-ESB.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250405134841)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ThereIsNoTry-ESB.flac "File:ThereIsNoTry-ESB.flac"))[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7)

Soon thereafter, Luke Skywalker, under guidance from the spirit of Kenobi, sought Yoda in his Dagobah exile to receive Jedi training.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7) At the same time, Yoda, stirred awake by the feeling of the dark side and the memories of his trauma years ago, went to his storage area to find it empty. In an effort to find food, he made the arduous trek across the wild terrain of Dagobah. Eventually, Yoda made it to a valley, full of colorful creatures, and another [species](/wiki/Unidentified_quadruped "Unidentified quadruped") in particular. Herds of these creatures ran through this valley, the best source of meat Yoda had yet been able to find.[[112]](#cite_note-Special_1-112)

 [![Luke Skywalker joins Yoda for dinner within the Jedi Master's hut.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/YodasHut-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250410034323) [![Luke Skywalker joins Yoda for dinner within the Jedi Master's hut.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/YodasHut-CGSWG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250410034323)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/YodasHut-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250410034323) 

Luke Skywalker joins Yoda for dinner within the Jedi Master's hut.

 

Years ago, Yoda in his shame had decided to give up his lightsaber, promising to never wield one again, taking a [bow](/wiki/Bow "Bow") instead. To get what he came for, Yoda readied his bow and took aim of one of the creatures, easily killing it with one shot of the bow. On his journey back, Yoda began to feel the ground shift beneath his feet, beginning to crumble as Yoda began to fall. At the last moment, Yoda grabbed onto the side, reflecting on the similarities of this moment to his duel with Darth Sidious many years ago. Yoda's grip failed and he falls onto the ground below as boulders began to pile on top of him. Yoda fell unconscious.[[112]](#cite_note-Special_1-112)

Yoda began to dream, the dream of pain, suffering, anger, hate, and suddenly, he awoke once again. Realizing the predicament he was in, Yoda began to laugh, laughing at his foolishness for allowing him to get into this situation. He began to doubt himself, thinking of how he was now trapped on Dagobah, but subsiding those feelings, knowing he was one of the last of the Jedi. He reached out to the Force and, in that moment, he realized that his shame, his hubris, his blindness, had all clouded his vision and realized his failings as a Jedi. However, he knew that failure was the greatest lesson a Jedi could learn, and understanding this brought him peace as he rejected allowing his shame to guide him any more. With this newfound peace, Yoda reattuned to the light and used its power to move the boulders resting on top of him. With a newfound sense of responsibility and understanding, Yoda began his journey home.[[112]](#cite_note-Special_1-112)

Arriving back at his home, Yoda began to cook a stew, when he began to hear a crashing in the [trees](/wiki/Tree "Tree") surrounding his hut. A visitor had arrived. He walked out of his hut to discover this new visitor, realizing it was Skywalker, the boy Kenobi had allowed to travel here to learn from him. As he stared at Skywalker from the trees, he came to the realization that he would not be the last Jedi, but only the instrument as to train the future.[[112]](#cite_note-Special_1-112)

 [![Yoda trains Luke Skywalker on Dagobah.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/There_Is_No_Try_WotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20191015020605) [![Yoda trains Luke Skywalker on Dagobah.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/There_Is_No_Try_WotF.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191015020605)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/There_Is_No_Try_WotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20191015020605) 

Yoda trains Luke Skywalker on Dagobah.

 

Walking out, he decided to test the boy and did not reveal his true identity, instead promising to lead him to Yoda. With Skywalker growing annoyed while in Yoda's hut as the Jedi Master made [rootleaf stew](/wiki/Rootleaf_stew "Rootleaf stew"), Skywalker's subsequent frustration and his age made the Jedi doubtful as to whether it was a good idea to train the boy, but Kenobi's spirit managed to convince him to do so.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7) Over the next few weeks, Yoda trained the young Jedi.[[118]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-118)

Yoda proceeded to tutor Skywalker with a variety of exercises, including the telekinetic manipulation of objects in the area. As part of his training, he also sent Skywalker into the dark side cave in order to [demonstrate](/wiki/Duel_on_Dagobah_(3_ABY) "Duel on Dagobah (3 ABY)") the dangers of falling to the dark side of the Force. During his tenure with Yoda, Skywalker sensed that his friends were in danger in [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City") on the [gas giant](/wiki/Gas_giant "Gas giant") Bespin, and headed there to confront Darth Vader in spite of Yoda's and Kenobi's persuasion to the contrary. Although Kenobi was distraught by Skywalker's rushed departure, Yoda reminded him that there was still another offspring of Anakin Skywalker[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7)—Leia Organa.[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119)

#### A disturbance in the Force

Sometime later, the same mysterious woman helped activate the [Fermata Cage](/wiki/Fermata_Cage "Fermata Cage"), a mysterious artifact created by [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin"). On her second attempt, Yoda along with other Force users amongst the galaxy sensed the disturbances emanating from the cage.[[120]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_2-120)

#### Death

:   "*Luke... when gone am I, the last of the Jedi, will you be. Luke... the Force runs strong in your family. Pass on what you have learned. Luke... There... is... another... Sk-... Sky... walker...*"
:   ―Yoda's last words, to Luke Skywalker[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119)

 [![Yoda becomes one with the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodasDeath-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20130402045854) [![Yoda becomes one with the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodasDeath-ROTJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130402045854)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodasDeath-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20130402045854) 

Yoda becomes one with the Force.

 

Skywalker, having engaged in a duel with Vader on Cloud City, returned to Dagobah after a year. Yoda,[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) ill and very close to death,[[5]](#cite_note-DatabankYoda-5) confirmed what Vader had revealed to the young Jedi on Bespin: that the Sith Lord indeed was Anakin Skywalker, his father. He also warned him that with his training fully complete, his final task would be confronting Vader again and defeating him, and cautioned Skywalker not to underestimate the Force powers of Galactic Emperor Darth Sidious. Yoda also said that when he dies, Luke will become the last of the Jedi. Therefore, he wanted Luke to pass on what he had learned. Finally, he also managed to inform him of the existence of another member of the Skywalker family. Yoda then died, and his body disappeared as he became one with the[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) light of the Force.[[20]](#cite_note-USWNE-20) The Cave of Evil took advantage of the Jedi Master's faltering presence and subsequent death to finally expand its influence once more, spreading a darkness across Dagobah.[[105]](#cite_note-Light_Falls-105)

### Postmortem and legacy

:   "*Heeded my words not, did you? Pass on what you have learned. Strength, mastery. But weakness… folly… failure, also. Yes, failure most of all. The greatest teacher, failure is. Luke… we are what they grow beyond. That is the true burden of all masters.*"
:   ―Yoda's Force spirit, to Luke Skywalker[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121)

 [![Anakin Skywalker, Yoda, and Obi-Wan Kenobi as Force spirits on Endor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) [![Anakin Skywalker, Yoda, and Obi-Wan Kenobi as Force spirits on Endor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20201008104501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) 

Anakin Skywalker, Yoda, and Obi-Wan Kenobi as Force spirits on Endor.

 

Thanks to the techniques passed on to him by Qui-Gon Jinn's spirit,[[5]](#cite_note-DatabankYoda-5) Yoda managed to retain his consciousness without a physical presence by becoming a Force spirit.[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) Mere moments after his death, he was able to appear to Sidious, who had felt his death in the Force. Sidious, who had been fantasizing about killing Yoda himself in the past few minutes as well as inwardly celebrating his demise, was surprised by Yoda's appearance, thinking the feat impossible. Putting on a show, he gloated on the fact that Yoda was now dead and implying that Yoda was there to witness Sidious' final glory as he crushed the remnants of the Rebel Alliance and took Luke Skywalker as his new apprentice. Yoda stressed that Sidious could not win, but Sidious pointed out that he already had. Awaiting Yoda's reply, Sidious discovered that his specter had vanished.[[122]](#cite_note-Masters-122)

Luke Skywalker later used the training he received to confront Darth Sidious and Darth Vader aboard the [DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") over the forest moon [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor") as part of an all-out attack on the station by the anti-Imperial [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"), defeating Vader and turning him back to the light side of the Force, resulting in Sidious' death at the hands of the redeemed Anakin Skywalker.[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) As Anakin died from his wounds, Yoda and Kenobi appeared to him, smiling upon their redeemed friend.[[123]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-123)

Yoda then taught Anakin the ability of retaining his consciousness after death.[[18]](#cite_note-AEYNTKUAE-18) As the rebels and Luke celebrated on the surface of the moon due to the demolition of the Death Star II and the deaths of Sidious and Vader, the ghosts of Anakin, Kenobi, and Yoda briefly appeared to Luke.[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) After that, Anakin asked Yoda and Kenobi whether Luke would be alright, and Kenobi responded as Yoda stood by.[[123]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-123) For the next years, Yoda's spirit, alongside Obi-Wan and Anakin, continued to guide Luke.[[124]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-124) Though it was rare, Yoda also spoke to Leia offering her guidance and teachings of the force over the years of her life, teachings she would later pass on to Rey.[[125]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-125)

Approximately five years after Yoda's passing,[[126]](#cite_note-Date_Note-126) the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") bounty hunter [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin") took a member of Yoda's species, [Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu"), to train under Ahsoka Tano on the planet of [Corvus](/wiki/Corvus "Corvus"). While with Djarin, Tano explained that she had only met one other member of Grogu's species: Master Yoda. Tano refused to train the Child but told Djarin that Grogu could reach out to other Jedi at the [seeing stone](/wiki/Seeing_stone "Seeing stone") on the planet of [Tython](/wiki/Tython "Tython").[[127]](#cite_note-Chapter13-127) Thus, Luke Skywalker learned of Grogu and, after [saving](/wiki/Second_rescue_of_Grogu "Second rescue of Grogu") Djarin, Grogu, and their allies from a [platoon](/wiki/Gideon%27s_Dark_Trooper_platoon "Gideon's Dark Trooper platoon") of [Dark Troopers](/wiki/Phase-III_Dark_Trooper "Phase-III Dark Trooper"), took Grogu as an apprentice.[[128]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-128) Thirty years after Yoda's death,[[3]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-3) another Force sensitive, [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), heard Yoda's voice describing the Force during a [vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") she witnessed upon touching the [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") that previously belonged to Luke and Anakin Skywalker.[[129]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-129)

 [![Yoda appears before Luke on Ahch-To.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/ArsonHaveICommitted-TLJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181122065145) [![Yoda appears before Luke on Ahch-To.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/ArsonHaveICommitted-TLJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20181122065145)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/ArsonHaveICommitted-TLJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181122065145) 

Yoda appears before Luke on Ahch-To.

 

Sometime later, and after Rey had visited Luke on his hermit-island on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"), a disillusioned and self-loathing Skywalker tried to burn down what few Jedi artifacts and writings were left in hopes that it would rid the galaxy of the Jedi once and for all, who, through him, had failed. Luke was surprised by the sudden appearance of Master Yoda as a Force spirit, who not only did not seem to mind the ancient scripts burning up, but was the one to actually start the fire by causing lightning to strike the tree. In fact, unbeknownst to Luke, Rey had already taken the [Sacred Jedi texts](/wiki/Sacred_Jedi_texts "Sacred Jedi texts") when she left. During their meeting, Yoda pointed out that mistakes and failure were important lessons, if not the most important lesson, for a Jedi Master. Ultimately, Yoda helped Skywalker come to terms with his failed training of [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), and to realize that despite his fear of failing another student he could still be what Rey needed. Inspiring Luke to face his past and forgive himself. This final, heartfelt meeting between the two friends led Luke to change his mind and help save the Resistance from certain defeat during the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait").[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121)

During the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"), Yoda's voice was heard by Rey among the voices of many Jedi of the past who aided her with destroying the resurrected Darth Sidious. "Alone, never have you been," he told her, before telling Rey to "rise in the Force."[[130]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-130)

## Personality and traits

:   "*You knew Master Yoda?*"  
    "*Yes. He taught almost all of the younglings in the temple, at one point or another.*"  
    "*Kanan described him to me. Small, green, and wrinkly with pointy ears. But he didn't know what he was really like.*"  
    "*I'm not sure anyone did. He was wise, kind, but when I was young, he seemed happier. As the Clone War dragged on, he carried a great burden, a deep sorrow, as if he knew before anyone else that one time was ending, and another beginning.*"
:   ―Ezra Bridger and Ahsoka Tano[[108]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-108)

 [![Yoda served as a teacher for the Jedi for 800 years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Yoda_teaching.png/revision/latest?cb=20121231133247) [![Yoda served as a teacher for the Jedi for 800 years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Yoda_teaching.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121231133247)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Yoda_teaching.png/revision/latest?cb=20121231133247) 

Yoda served as a teacher for the Jedi for 800 years.

 

Known for his wisdom, Yoda had spent eight centuries training and tutoring generations of Jedi.[[5]](#cite_note-DatabankYoda-5) Yoda was an ideal grandmaster.[[14]](#cite_note-Pocket_Expert-14) When he joined her Force-bond network, Jedi Master Avar Kriss felt Yoda's mind form its own part of the chorus of the Force. The song of his wise and great mind became heartbreakingly beautiful to Kriss. Despite his appearance not making it seem like it would be so, his voice appeared to be made up of pure light, so Kriss considered him the epitome that people were not simply the crude matter of their bodies,[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26) a lesson that Yoda would later pass on to Luke Skywalker.[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) He was reluctant to accept Anakin Skywalker or Luke Skywalker for Jedi training, considering them unfit. In both cases, however, he allowed Obi-Wan Kenobi to persuade him into accepting them as trainees.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_I-9)[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119)

Yoda understood that nothing and no one was perfect, but that there was good or the potential for good everywhere and in everything. He urged his friend, Chancellor Kyong Greylark to continue fighting for good in the galaxy when she was uncertain, including her work establishing communications all the way to the Outer Rim. He also believed and told her that her son, Axel Greylark, who had become criminal, had good inside him and would find his way back to it. Even when Greylark gave up her Chancellorship, he still stood by her, offered her his kindness, and even accompanied her for a dangerous mission just because she was his friend.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

There was a small garden in the Jedi Temple where Yoda often took to meditating, with the other Jedi usually respecting the privacy of such moments. Indeed, Yoda's favorite place to be was his own thoughts, being able to meditate and feel the calm [Living Force](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force") flow throughout him.[[65]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-65) When Dooku triggered a partial room collapse during his duel with Yoda on Geonosis, the Jedi, confronted with the choice of pursuing the fleeing Sith or protecting the hurt Obi-Wan Kenobi and unconscious Anakin Skywalker from the falling debris, opting to save his comrades instead of going after Dooku.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) However, when fellow Master Plo Koon's fleet was destroyed by the Confederate superweapon *Malevolence*, Yoda forbade Anakin Skywalker and Ahsoka Tano to conduct a search for Koon, citing the danger posed by the Separatist vessel.[[82]](#cite_note-TCW:RM-82) Early in the Clone Wars, after learning he would be confronting Dooku's apprentice Asajj Ventress during his mission on Rugosa, Yoda was disappointed to not be facing the Count himself, believing that he could end the bloodshed by meeting with Dooku; Yoda believed he could connect with his former Padawan and redeem him to the light side of the Force.[[23]](#cite_note-L&D-23) Later in the war, however, Yoda reluctantly agreed to a plan to assassinate Dooku in the name of stopping the war. Obi-Wan Kenobi, after the plan's failure, would argue to his fellow councilmembers the mission had been a step too far into the dark.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

Padawan Reath Silas believed that having Yoda as a master would be "pretty fun" whilst discussing Yoda's former apprentice Kantam Sy.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25) Yoda's favorite method of teaching was to ensure his students could figure things out for themselves. Even if all Yoda did was wait for the student to catch up to speed, he found that they almost always realized what they needed. When Master Mace Windu questioned whether Yoda had sensed something or not, he waited until the younger Jedi realized he was sensing nothing. Windu remained confused, forcing him to explain that the feeling of nothing needed to be caused by something. He disagreed with Windu's sentiment that "nothing" and "something" were always opposites, and he made sure to never be fully sure of himself, knowing there was more to learn. Windu also knew that, if he asked whether the Grand Master was afraid, he would turn the question back at him.[[65]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-65)

Yoda remained calm even when insulted, such as when the mud dwellers called him a "weird little frog".[[131]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_27-131) During the Invasion of Naboo, Yoda believed himself comfortably away from the dark side, unaware of the growing power of Darth Sidious, with the exception of what he knew he could not feel. Indeed, Yoda concerned himself with trying to uncover the feelings that were hidden from his senses,[[65]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-65) which he eventually understood to be the dark side.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) Yoda was able to resist being tempted by the specter of the dead Sith Lord Darth Bane, who had appeared to him in a vision on the planet Moraband, recognizing that the spirit was a mere illusion and rejecting its call to the dark side.[[96]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-96) However, he was quite concerned and worried about the danger and threat of the Nameless, which he secretly knew of quite well, opting to keep information about them out of the Jedi Archives so that they would not be known and used against the Order.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31)

 [![Wise yet old, Yoda spent his final years on Dagobah, training Luke Skywalker and coming to terms with his own mortality.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/BountyHunters-4-Sprouse-textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20210523170546) [![Wise yet old, Yoda spent his final years on Dagobah, training Luke Skywalker and coming to terms with his own mortality.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/BountyHunters-4-Sprouse-textless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20210523170546)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/BountyHunters-4-Sprouse-textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20210523170546) 

Wise yet old, Yoda spent his final years on Dagobah, training Luke Skywalker and coming to terms with his own mortality.

 

Yoda's teachings stuck with his students, even if at times they had to struggle to understand their true meaning. Upon hearing pilot [Leox Gyasi](/wiki/Leox_Gyasi "Leox Gyasi") explain why he had named his starship "the *[Vessel](/wiki/Vessel "Vessel")*," Silas was struck with the opinion that Gyasi sounded like what Yoda's teachings would be like if the Jedi Master took [spice](/wiki/Spice "Spice"). As such, Silas decided his reasoning was either a very good or extremely bad sign.[[132]](#cite_note-Into_the_Dark-132) Despite barely knowing the Grand Master, Silas was greatly struck by his disappearance during the High Republic Era, with fellow Padawan [Ram Jomaram](/wiki/Ram_Jomaram "Ram Jomaram"), despite having never even met Yoda, agreeing and feeling the same.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25) As he neared his death before the Battle of Endor commenced, Yoda accepted his own mortality and imminent demise and died becoming one with the Force.[[5]](#cite_note-DatabankYoda-5) Yoda's [ears](/wiki/Ear "Ear") were expressive and would sometimes curl when he was expressing strong emotions like surprise.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8) These ears were also highly sensitive[[1]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-1) and also sometimes would move to express his emotions.[[14]](#cite_note-Pocket_Expert-14) The Grandmaster preferred to not kill his enemies if it was not needed, if he had the opportunity to resolve a fight by disarming or overawing his foes. Yoda opposed profanity, urging others to not use such language.[[133]](#cite_note-Yoda_1-133)

Yoda also had a sense of humor and curiosity, despite his age and wisdom.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7) Part of the reason Yoda kept up his sense of humor was that Jedi Master Mace Windu, even as a youngling, did not respond well to it. As such, he took teasing his fellow council member, once asking if he had arrived for a private discussion because he had embarrassing questions, which Windu denied instantly. Afterward, he elected to wait to speak, wanting Windu to begin the discussion and viewing it as him cracking as if he was under pressure. Windu also found Yoda's behaviors distracting, yet he would always trust the older Jedi's judgement[[65]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-65) and he himself described Yoda as "hilarious".[[134]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_3-134) His sense of humor continued with others, as shown when he playfully rummaged through Luke's belongings when he first met him, fought R2-D2 for a torch,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7) and laughed gleefully when he supposedly set the ancient Jedi texts on fire, and finding Luke's continued ignorance amusing, commenting that he had "missed him."[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121) Also when Kenobi told him about the planet Kamino missing from the archives during his class, he responded with, "Lost a planet, Master Kenobi has. How embarrassing. How embarrassing!"[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) Being unable to destroy Darth Sidious and bring down the Empire made him sad.[[135]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Jedi_Pocket_Expert-135)[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10)

Yoda was highly secretive about his homeworld and never revealed it to anyone.[[1]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-1) Despite his intensive Jedi training and high status within the Order, he stated that he secretly had a dislike for ancient Jedi texts.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121) He had a distinctive and peculiar speech pattern: namely, he would rearrange words in his sentences, placing subject and object in front of the verb; for example, he would frame sentences like "Good relations with the Wookiees, I have."[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10)

## Powers and abilities

 [![Yoda was one of the most proficient Jedi with the lightsaber.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/TCW-BattleTales-1-Momoko.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200602001403) [![Yoda was one of the most proficient Jedi with the lightsaber.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/TCW-BattleTales-1-Momoko.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20200602001403)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/TCW-BattleTales-1-Momoko.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200602001403) 

Yoda was one of the most proficient Jedi with the lightsaber.

 

### Lightsaber combat

:   "*It is obvious that this contest cannot be decided by our knowledge of the Force…but by our skills with a lightsaber.*"
:   ―Dooku, to Yoda[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15)

Despite his small size and old age, Yoda was an extremely accomplished lightsaber duelist, wielding a short green-bladed lightsaber.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10)[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) Yoda used the [Ataru](/wiki/Form_IV "Form IV") saber form, boosting his body with the Force to be able to perform the needed movements.[[136]](#cite_note-Knights_of_Fate-136) Such was his mastery of this form that Yoda could duel Sidious and almost defeated the Sith.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10) Yoda was a master of the [Niman](/wiki/Form_VI "Form VI") style of lightsaber combat, retaining his skills with the form for his whole life.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137)

Yoda was extremely skilled in blast-deflection and proved more than capable of taking on multiple enemies at the same time and winning easily: he was able to single-handedly defeat without getting even a single shot to his person an entire army of droids that Ventress sent as a test for King Katunko whether to accept the Jedi or the Separatists as an ally.[[77]](#cite_note-TCW:Ambush-77)

The greatest display of Yoda's skills with a lightsaber was when he dueled the Sith Lords Count Dooku[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) and Darth Sidious. When he fought Dooku, Yoda maintained the upper hand through the duel, forcing Dooku into the defensive, and would have defeated him had he not decided to flee. His duel with Sidious, although initially well-matched, eventually began to turn into Yoda's favor, forcing Sidious to use the Force to confront him.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10)

### Force powers

:   "*The history of a soul, does the Force permit* me *to understand.*"
:   ―Yoda about his abilities[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

Even despite his small size and old age, Yoda was extremely powerful and accomplished in the Force. with a connection to that power and knowledge of [Force techniques](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") that may well have surpassed that of any other Jedi.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7)[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) Obi-Wan Kenobi considered Yoda to be the most powerful Jedi he ever knew.[[131]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_27-131) The Grandmaster was heralded as the greatest Jedi of all time, at least until the fall of the Republic. Yoda was utterly committed to the light side, but he also had a deep understanding of the dark side as well as how both halves of the Force interacted.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) The idea he was the greatest of the Jedi went back centuries, at being held least to 232 BBY.[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26)[[138]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Timelines-138) The toll age took on Yoda's body did not prevent him from still being strong in the Force when Luke Skywalker trained under him.[[124]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-124) Even in death, as a Force spirit, he had power over weather.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121)

 [![Yoda uses the Force to lift Skywalker's X-wing out of the Dagobah swamp.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Do_or_Do_Not_SWDTPG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190428031515) [![Yoda uses the Force to lift Skywalker's X-wing out of the Dagobah swamp.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Do_or_Do_Not_SWDTPG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190428031515)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Do_or_Do_Not_SWDTPG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190428031515) 

Yoda uses the Force to lift Skywalker's X-wing out of the Dagobah swamp.

 

Yoda was extremely skilled in [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") and all forms of it. When Avar Kriss worked with the other Jedi to shove a sun-bursting explosive Avar Kriss found his level of power (which he lent via her Force Song) to be very grand, helpful, and impressive.[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26) When on a mission to free a child, Yoda gripped two pirates who were holding the child and held them helpless, before making them punch each other and then threw them into the air. Then Yoda defeated the rest of the pirates in the room when they attacked him.[[139]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-139) Yoda used Force deflection against a [Blue stone](/wiki/Blue_stone "Blue stone") spear thrown at him by a member of the [Mud dwellers](/wiki/Mud_dwellers "Mud dwellers"), though holding the spear with the Force was hard for Yoda. Yoda then levitated many boulders and rocks to catch the rest of the spears thrown at him and kept the rocks levitated for a whole conversation. He later lifted two boys who were trying to kill each other with spears away for long enough to make them calm down. Yoda was unable to [repel](/wiki/Force_deflection "Force deflection") many of the [Blue stones](/wiki/Blue_stone "Blue stone") that were thrown at him with the Force by the [Rockhawkers](/wiki/Rockhawkers "Rockhawkers"), due to how hard it was to affect with telekinesis and his unwillingness to harm the [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") he faced.[[131]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_27-131) Later, and having mastered [Stonepower](/wiki/Stonepower "Stonepower"), Yoda was able to casually blast the Rockhawkers who attacked him, subduing and disarming them without inflicting lasting harm.[[12]](#cite_note-SW_30-12)

When facing Dooku on the planet Geonosis, Yoda demonstrated his superior telekinetic mastery by effortlessly repelling every metal piece and stone slab thrown by the very skilled Sith Lord. During a confrontation with Confederate forces on the coral moon of Rugosa, Yoda effortlessly pulled two droids to slash them with his lightsaber, flung multiple pieces of the droid controlling one of the infantry high into the air and both opened the upper parts of another infantry tank, then sent it and the droid controlling it into the air. It was with ease that Yoda raised and moved droids to fire upon their allies and slammed whole squads of droids down, without harming his own allies. After the droids were dealt with, Yoda easily overpowered the powerful Sith Assassin [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") with telekinesis, stopping her lightsaber strike mid-way and disarming her with a simple gesture, and repulsed the many stones caused by Ventress activating an explosion.[[77]](#cite_note-TCW:Ambush-77) If Yoda had no desire to touch the ground, he could simply [float](/wiki/Levitation "Levitation") in a mediative state.[[140]](#cite_note-Battlefront-140)

[Force barriers](/wiki/Force_barrier "Force barrier") were a tool in Yoda's skill set, as seen when he stopped a cloud of deadly gas.[[86]](#cite_note-ZBSB-86) Yoda could strike down his foes by hurling his saber at them, guiding the blow with his telekinetic skills. When he went to try to destroy the Sith Emperor, Yoda effortlessly defeated two Red Guards by knocking them into a wall. He was even able to breach the Emperor's defenses and blast Darth Sidious himself through the air with a [Force push](/wiki/Force_push "Force push") and was able to stop and throw a Senate hoverpod Sidious had thrown at him when they fought in the Senate building, an all the more impressive feat since it was thrown upwards against gravity.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10) Later, on Dagobah, Yoda used the Force to throw a pot at an Imperial Probe Droid, destroying it. He then [Force crushed](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") two more of the robots before they could report his location.[[106]](#cite_note-FACPOV-106) In order to teach Luke Skywalker that anything was possible with the Force, Yoda levitated his student's sunken [T-65B X-wing starfighter](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter") out of a swamp of Dagobah and onto dry land with no visible strain.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7)

With just a few days of training, Yoda was able to learn how to use [Stonepower](/wiki/Stonepower "Stonepower") and thus deflect Blue stones thrown at him. Yoda could move a chunk three times his size--something unknown to his master, though Yoda was then exhausted by doing so.[[141]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_28-141) Yoda could also use Stonepower to stop strikes from [giants of living stone](/wiki/Giants_of_living_stone "Giants of living stone"), and with the aid of those he taught, call forth other giants to defeat the one he was fighting.[[12]](#cite_note-SW_30-12) Yoda was capable of employing the power of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"), to the point that he could make several arcs of energy lance out in different directions from only a single finger.[[142]](#cite_note-Unlimited_Power-142) Yoda could manipulate [flames](/wiki/Fire "Fire") with the Force.[[141]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_28-141)

Jedi Padawan [Bell Zettifar](/wiki/Bell_Zettifar "Bell Zettifar") pondered whether Yoda, after putting great focus into the effort, could use the Force to stop gravity.[[26]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-26) In his duel with both Sith Lords Count Dooku and Darth Sidious, Yoda displayed great proficiency in [Force Deflection](/wiki/Force_deflection "Force deflection"), as he was able to easily stop and then redirect Dooku's Force lightning attack with his bare hands and even managed to stop Sidious' Force lightning attack using just his palms but was unable to deflect it completely: the energy eventually exploded and flung both of the combatants away from each other, ending the duel in a stalemate and causing Yoda to escape.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10) Yoda could dampen or even negate the might of Force powers used to attack him by radiating a calming aura.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) Yoda could employ the Force to absorb blaster fire and negate the strikes of lightsabers with his bare hands and channel the energy from blasters or lightning he absorbed into making his own attacks such as Force push and Force lightning more deadly.[[140]](#cite_note-Battlefront-140)

 [![Yoda was capable of absorbing and deflecting Force lightning with his palms.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Yodasforcedeflection.png/revision/latest?cb=20130205191709) [![Yoda was capable of absorbing and deflecting Force lightning with his palms.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Yodasforcedeflection.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130205191709)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Yodasforcedeflection.png/revision/latest?cb=20130205191709) 

Yoda was capable of absorbing and deflecting Force lightning with his palms.

 

His ability to use the combative applications of the Force notwithstanding, Yoda's incredibly strong connection to the Force combined with his years of extensive study also granted him numerous supplementary abilities. Yoda could enhance himself and seek out objects or persons he knew about regardless of the distance, and easily see though and/or destroy many Force illusions at once.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) During the trial of [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos"), Yoda revealed that he could uncover the alignment of a Force-user just by touching them; stating that the Force had permitted him to read the history of a soul, able to easily sense that he had fallen to the Dark Side despite Vos being proficient enough to hide it from many other Jedi.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8) Yoda could detect the lies, emotional states, and thoughts of those he interacted with.[[131]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_27-131)[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137)

While physically isolated on Dagobah, Yoda was able to see other Jedi that were active in the Force; he could not see one that had forsaken the ways of the Jedi, with the exception of Vader who was still exposed to his monitoring.[[143]](#cite_note-Video-143)[[106]](#cite_note-FACPOV-106) Yoda could detect living things and droids with the Force and while on Dagobah he could sense all droids on the entire planet or the lack thereof.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137)[[23]](#cite_note-L&D-23) He could keep in mental contact with the Jedi Temples across the galaxy, and [telepathically](/wiki/Telepathy "Telepathy") converse with any Jedi–even to the point of manipulating the experience to his desires–within them by accessing the [World Between Worlds](/wiki/World_Between_Worlds "World Between Worlds").[[111]](#cite_note-POTJ-111)[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) Yoda, still on Dagobah, was able to conjure an illusion of the Grand Inquisitor (from when he was a Jedi) to fight Kanan Jarrus as a test and sight of worthiness. He also sensed that the place where Ezra Bridger and Kanan Jarrus could be assured of a chance to fight the Sith was Malachor, and so told Ezra. When the [Lothal Jedi Temple](/wiki/Lothal_Jedi_Temple "Lothal Jedi Temple") was invaded, Yoda sent illusions of Jedi Temple Guards at the Inquisitors, subduing them for long enough for the living Jedi present to flee.[[108]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-108)

With some effort, Yoda could make himself and the powers he invoked impossible to detect with the Force and go unnoticed by most.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) When two Blue stone spears were struck together, Yoda sensed the [disturbance](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force") this caused.[[139]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-139) He also sensed the killings that took place during Order 66, the shock of which literarily staggered him, so forewarned by the Force, Yoda was able to destroy the Clones soon sent to slay him on behalf of the Sith.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_III-10) He also was able to sense when a battle was going to happen, getting an identifiable feeling that he felt shortly before the Night of Sorrow.[[31]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-31) Yoda could use the Force to see even in total darkness or when blinded.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) Additionally, Yoda was able to use [Force healing](/wiki/Force_healing "Force healing"), even to the extent of healing himself and those around him while in battle with just a wave of his hand.[[140]](#cite_note-Battlefront-140)[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) Yoda was also shown to be capable of experiencing Force visions and could invoke such insights at will for information up to three days into his personal future.[[137]](#cite_note-Allies-137) However, he understood that Force prophecy was not absolute and that the future was always in motion.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_V-7) The Grandmaster could make [great leaps](/wiki/Force_jump "Force jump") with the Force, to maneuver and dodge[[77]](#cite_note-TCW:Ambush-77) and charge.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_II-15) His visions led him to foresee the possible, and eventually actual, fall of the Jedi in the Clone Wars and even his own [death](/wiki/Death "Death").[[96]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-96) Yoda sometimes knew if he was probably going to die in a battle he fought in and could augment his physical abilities.[[12]](#cite_note-SW_30-12)

He also was able to fully master the skill of [maintaining consciousness after death](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit"), something that Qui-Gon Jinn was unable to do, allowing him to manifest a visible presence rather than simply being a disembodied voice.[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-119) As a Force spirit, Yoda was capable of manipulating weather to create lightning strikes. He was also shown to be capable of striking Luke Skywalker with his walking stick, demonstrating an ability to interact with the living world in a physical sense despite both Yoda and the stick being ostensibly non-corporeal.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121)

### Other skills

 [![Yoda takes control of his personal Jedi interceptor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Yoda_starfighter_Voices.png/revision/latest?cb=20150413050015) [![Yoda takes control of his personal Jedi interceptor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Yoda_starfighter_Voices.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20150413050015)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Yoda_starfighter_Voices.png/revision/latest?cb=20150413050015) 

Yoda takes control of his personal Jedi interceptor.

 

Yoda was also known to have a level of proficiency in piloting[[139]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-139) despite often leaving it to his soldiers, as when he was forced to travel alone by Qui-Gon Jinn, Yoda displayed the ability to pilot Anakin's personal interceptor comfortably and was able to avoid inflicting any damage on it until he returned to the Jedi.[[95]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-95)[[57]](#cite_note-Destiny-57)[[96]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-96) Sidious and Yoda were equally matched during their duel in the Galactic Senate.[[1]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-1)

According to Obi-Wan, Yoda's thirst for knowledge was the grandmaster's greatest weapon. Yoda could walk for hours without food or rest up a mountain/giant.[[141]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_28-141) Padawan Reath Silas once reflected that he could feel Yoda's wisdom and knowledge from even a [kilometer](/wiki/Kilometer "Kilometer") away.[[25]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-25)

During the Clone Wars, Yoda proved himself to be an exceptional strategist and leader, being a highly effective general. His abilities in those regard were displayed during a confrontation with Confederate forces on the coral moon of Rugosa: Yoda was able to inspire hope into his troopers despite the overwhelming odds and was able to easily tactically defeat the army of droids, exploiting the weak-points of the infantry and tanks to systematically destroy them and at one point tricking one of the droids controlling the tanks into destroying the other tank.[[77]](#cite_note-TCW:Ambush-77)

Yoda was a skilled diplomat.[[77]](#cite_note-TCW:Ambush-77) Although his cooking on Dagobah left much to be desired,[[118]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-118) Yoda was skilled at baking, with Jedi Master Torban Buck particularly enjoying Yoda's pastry recipe.[[45]](#cite_note-HRA_4-45)

## Equipment

:   "*I am knowledgeable of many things. But I have never worn shoes!*"
:   ―Yoda[[144]](#cite_note-Living_Force-144)

 [![Yoda could appear as an elder figure one moment and then an agile lightsaber wielder the next.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/TheHighRepublicEdgeOfBalancePremonition-reveal-cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240722161454) [![Yoda could appear as an elder figure one moment and then an agile lightsaber wielder the next.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/TheHighRepublicEdgeOfBalancePremonition-reveal-cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240722161454)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/TheHighRepublicEdgeOfBalancePremonition-reveal-cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240722161454) 

Yoda could appear as an elder figure one moment and then an agile lightsaber wielder the next.

 

Throughout the Republic Era, Yoda wielded a [shoto](/wiki/Shoto_lightsaber "Shoto lightsaber")-style [lightsaber](/wiki/Yoda%27s_lightsaber "Yoda's lightsaber"), although he lost it in a duel with Darth Sidious at the end of the Clone Wars. He kept a [near identical lightsaber](/wiki/Yoda%27s_second_lightsaber "Yoda's second lightsaber") with him on Dagobah. He was also known for using a cane. It began as a lesson, but really more of a joke, for his Padawans; he would limp into a room with the cane, then he would cast it aside and quickly use his speed in the Force, only to finally grab the cane once more and hobble away. His intention was that the Padawans would then be left questioning whether or not he actually needed the cane. Nevertheless, as he grew older during his exile on Dagobah, he found he truly had come to need it.[[106]](#cite_note-FACPOV-106)

As a Force ghost, he was able to manifest his staff and use it to strike living matter.[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121) His cane was made from a [Gimer stick](/wiki/Gimer_stick "Gimer stick"), which released natural plant substances that helped him meditate when he chewed upon it. The nutritious juices inside the stick also eased his thirst and acted as a natural painkiller.[[18]](#cite_note-AEYNTKUAE-18)

## Behind the scenes

### The Original trilogy

:   "*The idea of using another person, perhaps an alien, for Luke to play off of came up during story meetings. George Lucas and Leigh Brackett thought that the alien could be an Indian desert type, very childlike even though he's an old man. He at first should be repulsive and slimy but then should become kind and wise. He appears as a crazy little nitwit that goes around scurrying like a rat but ultimately teaches Luke a great deal about the Force.*"
:   ―[Laurent Bouzereau](/wiki/Laurent_Bouzereau "Laurent Bouzereau") about Yoda's development for Episode V[[145]](#cite_note-Annotated-145)

 [![Early concept art by .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Grand_Old_Wizard.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230614034216) [![Early concept art by .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Grand_Old_Wizard.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230614034216)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Grand_Old_Wizard.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230614034216) 

Early concept art by [Joe Johnston](/wiki/Joe_Johnston "Joe Johnston").

 

The character of Yoda made his first appearance in the [1980](/wiki/1980 "1980") film [*Star Wars*: Episode V *The Empire Strikes Back*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_V_The_Empire_Strikes_Back "Star Wars: Episode V The Empire Strikes Back"), and subsequently appeared in [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"), the closing installment of the original trilogy. He was also featured in all three episodes of the prequel trilogy, and multiple episodes of the *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* and *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")* animated television series. Yoda also played a role in various Expanded Universe material now under the [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") brand and thus [non-canonical](/wiki/Canon "Canon").[[146]](#cite_note-canon-146) In [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas")' notes for the [first chapter](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope") of the original trilogy Yoda originally named as "Bunden Debannen" and nicknamed as "Buffy". During the development of the sequel, Lucas, likening the character to "a little [Dalai Lama](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dalai_Lama "wikipedia:Dalai Lama")", decided to use an eastern sounding name and changed the character's name to "Minch Yoda" in the resultant treatment before simply shortened it to "Yoda" for the final film.[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147)[[148]](#cite_note-The_Making_of_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-148)

Much of the information and training that Yoda gave to Luke on Dagobah was originally going to be given by [Ben Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), but due to Kenobi's death in *A New Hope*, [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") conceived Yoda to fulfill the role of Luke's teacher after Kenobi's death.[[149]](#cite_note-FStJ:_TMoS-149) Early concepts of Yoda imagined him as a large alien before he was reimplemented as a tiny one, with various gnome– and elfin-like portrayals being created by the design team of Episode V. Once Yoda's appearance was finalized, make-up and creatures supervisor [Stuart Freeborn](/wiki/Stuart_Freeborn "Stuart Freeborn")[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147) sculpted[[150]](#cite_note-Archive_227-150) a detailed puppet, brought to life on screen by [Frank Oz](/wiki/Frank_Oz "Frank Oz").[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147) Every time that Oz turned the puppet, the ears would do a little wiggle, which he did not like. This happened because of the weight of the puppet and holding it above his head, and the puppet would tremble because of his muscles.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151)

While Yoda was largely depicted with the Oz-performed puppet in *The Empire Strikes Back*, actor [Deep Roy](/wiki/Deep_Roy "Deep Roy") stepped in for long shots of Yoda walking through the swamps. For these shots, Roy wore a detailed mask and full costume.[[150]](#cite_note-Archive_227-150) Yoda had additional play in the draft script for *Return of the Jedi*: when Emperor Palpatine strikes at Luke Skywalker with Force lightning aboard Death Star II, the Force ghost of Yoda would have appeared alongside the ghost of Kenobi. Both Jedi would have deflected the Emperor's lightning to protect Luke. Like Anakin Skywalker and Kenobi did in the draft, Yoda also returned to life instead of remaining a ghost.[[152]](#cite_note-Rewind_of_the_Jedi-152)

### The Prequel trilogy

:   "*I thought, 'I don't want to be matching to the puppet.' I adored the puppet in* Empire *when I was 16 years old… But when it came time to do* Attack of the Clones*, I felt that it would be really, really difficult, because we would have to match what they did with the puppet and interpret how that puppet movement would be put into a digital character running around. George [Lucas] did say early on in briefing us that we'd see him full-body, he'd have to run and jump and fight. So I did know that, but I thought after learning what we learned on Watto, Jar Jar, and Sebulba [in Episode I], I felt we could take on Yoda.*"
:   ―Rob Coleman discussing creating a digital Yoda for Episode II[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151)

A new model, younger in appearance, was built by [Nick Dudman](/wiki/Nick_Dudman "Nick Dudman")'s animatronics crew for the filming of Episode I, in which Yoda also appeared as a CGI model for two shots' duration.[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147) In Episode II, Yoda needed to be more agile than he was in the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") and would have to fight[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) during his duel with Dooku,[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147) which was a creative risk for the film. Initially, Lucas told Animation Director [Rob Coleman](/wiki/Rob_Coleman "Rob Coleman") that Yoda would be featured as a puppet and the animators would create a digital version of him for his duel with Count Dooku, but Coleman did not love the idea. He thought that it would be very difficult to match what was done for the Yoda puppet in *The Empire Strikes Back* and interpret how the puppet's movement would be put into a digital character. Early on in briefing, Lucas told Coleman and his team that Yoda would be seen full-body and he would have to run, jump, and fight. Coleman felt like he and his team could work on Yoda after gaining knowledge and experience from working on [Watto](/wiki/Watto "Watto"), [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks"), and [Sebulba](/wiki/Sebulba "Sebulba") in *The Phantom Menace*. The new goal was to use a digital Yoda for every scene and sequence that he appeared in.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) Designed specifically to not exceed Oz's puppetwork in realism, the animated version of Yoda was accepted after Coleman's crew secretly developed animation tests using key scenes from *The Empire Strikes Back* using the new technology, and these scenes were evaluated. Based on the strength of these animated tests, Coleman's crew was given permission to create a digital Yoda, which was realized entirely through computer-generated imagery.[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147)

Creating a digital Yoda terrified Coleman because of the backlash against Jar Jar, and he did not want to be known for "wrecking" Yoda, but he was unwilling to back down from a challenge. Coleman's memory of seeing Yoda in 1980 managed to keep him on target. Coleman studied the footage of Yoda in the *Empire Strikes Back* frame by frame and realized it was very limited. When creating the digital Yoda, he wanted himself and his team to honor the range of motion he thought he saw in 1980. Coleman pitched that the digital Yoda would do three talking shots[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) while delivering memorable lines of dialogue,[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147) as well as three shots without talking[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) to show the ability to convey a performance even when silent.[[147]](#cite_note-DB:Yoda-147) Coleman worked on a closeup of Yoda for the film in which Palpatine was speaking to Jedi in his office, and Lucas purposefully cut to Yoda who was looking over his shoulder. This was meant to indicate that Yoda did not trust Palpatine.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151)

Coleman worked with Frank Oz in order to make sure that his digital Yoda could be as faithful as possile. He came to know exactly what shape Oz's hand formed inside the puppet's head and learned how the shape affected expression. Coleman made sure that he did not go too far in terms of Yoda's movement. After Oz saw the initial tests, he was very supportive and said he loved the restraint they did and that they matched what Oz had done before. At first, the digital character did not include the original detail of how Yoda's ears wiggled everytime the puppet's head moved. This caused Yoda to not appear old, which was considered to be a vital part of his character. Coleman's team added the detail in the digital character, and Yoda now looked the correct age.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151)

From the start of the creation of Yoda and Count Dooku's lightsaber duel, most of the work would fall to Coleman's team. He did not get the script until he had been in [Sydney](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sydney "wikipedia:Sydney"), [Australia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia "wikipedia:Australia") for one or two [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week"). The first draft described the fight as "'In a fight that defies description, Yoda and Count Dooku battle." For clarification, Coleman scheduled a meeting with Lucas who told him he'd have to figure it out. To do this, Coleman went to stunt coordinator [Nick Gillard](/wiki/Nick_Gillard "Nick Gillard") and they talked about how a combatant would fight with small [weapons](/wiki/Weapon "Weapon"), and they looked at real-world examples. Also, [Ahmed Best](/wiki/Ahmed_Best "Ahmed Best"), the actor who played Jar Jar, introduced Coleman to some [anime](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anime "wikipedia:Anime")[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) and [martial arts](/wiki/Unarmed_combat "Unarmed combat")[[153]](#cite_note-Ahmed_Best_help-153) that he thought could be helpful. However, Coleman still was not sure how to depict Yoda's speed and style in a fight. He attended a screening of the [1992](/wiki/1992 "1992") film, [Swordsman II](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swordsman_II "wikipedia:Swordsman II") and one of the scenes showed [ninjas](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ninja "wikipedia:Ninja") leaping between [trees](/wiki/Tree "Tree") and bouncing around.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) Coleman studied the action in the film,[[153]](#cite_note-Ahmed_Best_help-153) and this inspired him to give Yoda the ability to jump around.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151) While working on the duel, Coleman referred to [Glen McIntosh](/wiki/Glen_McIntosh "Glen McIntosh")'s dynamic drawings.[[153]](#cite_note-Ahmed_Best_help-153) In the duel, Lucas wanted a shot of Yoda pulling back his duster to reveal his lightsaber as a reference to the iconic shot of the [gunfighter at the O.K Corral](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gunfight_at_the_O.K._Corral "wikipedia:Gunfight at the O.K. Corral"). After finishing the duel, Lucas and Coleman felt happy with it. Despite Coleman's concerns, Lucas wanted Yoda to jump, leap, and flip during the duel.[[151]](#cite_note-Clones_at_20-151)

Coleman worked on a shot that was called "The Widowmaker." In the shot, an animated Yoda denounced Kenobi's sense of victory and said "Begun, this Clone War has." That line was approved and unapproved a couple of times. Also, Coleman received many notes telling him the line had to be sadder. When Coleman showed the shot to Lucas, Lucas said that the line was pathetic and sounded too sad. Lucas said Yoda should not sound sad, and should instead sound reflective, concerned, and upset over the inevitability of the Clone Wars.[[154]](#cite_note-Yoda_sad-154)

For Episode III, the shot of Yoda clinging to the Senate podium during his duel with Sidious was animated by [Tim Harrington](/wiki/Tim_Harrington "Tim Harrington"). Coleman thought that his blocking was excellent, but Coleman was looking for more strain on Yoda's face. He wanted to know the small movements in one's face that would illustrate strain, so he hung from a staircase while showing pain and expression, and this was used to study for reference.[[155]](#cite_note-Yoda_strain-155)

### Animated television shows

Yoda's *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* and *[Star Wars Forces of Destiny](/wiki/Star_Wars_Forces_of_Destiny "Star Wars Forces of Destiny")* incarnation was voiced by veteran *Star Wars* voice actor [Tom Kane](/wiki/Tom_Kane "Tom Kane").[[156]](#cite_note-Kane-Interview-156) During the *Revenge of the Sith* DVD press conference in [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005"), Oz initially mentioned that he was going to be involved in the *Clone Wars* series, but in a [2007](/wiki/2007 "2007") interview with Aintitcoolnews.com he eventually denied any involvement.[[157]](#cite_note-Hyperspace-157) In spite of this, Oz later returned to voice the character in *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")*. [Piotr Michael](/wiki/Piotr_Michael "Piotr Michael") provided the voice for *[Star Wars: Young Jedi Adventures](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Young_Jedi_Adventures "Star Wars: Young Jedi Adventures")*.

### The Sequel trilogy

:   "*Neal Scanlan and his team did a recreation of the Yoda puppet. It's not only a puppet, it's an exact replica of the* Empire *puppet. They found the original molds for it. They found the woman that painted the original eyes for Yoda. Then Frank came and worked with them for a few weeks to get the puppet right. He did a lot of testing and a lot of adjusting with the puppet creators. It was amazing to watch the process.*"
:   ―Rian Johnson[[158]](#cite_note-158)

Oz continued to perform as Yoda in all three films of the [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"): the [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015") film [*Star Wars*: Episode VII *The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens"),[[159]](#cite_note-159) the [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017") film [*Star Wars*: Episode VIII *The Last Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VIII_The_Last_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi"),[[121]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-121) and the [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019") film [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker").[[130]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-130) In *The Force Awakens*, Yoda's voice was heard during Rey's Force vision along with Obi-Wan Kenobi's. During the film's early development, Yoda was originally going to have a bigger role, a decision that went far enough to ask Frank Oz to record some lines as Yoda, although these recordings went unused when the character was cut from the film.[[160]](#cite_note-EP7_Cut-160) *The Last Jedi* director [Rian Johnson](/wiki/Rian_Johnson "Rian Johnson") praised the development process for Yoda's appearance in the film.[[161]](#cite_note-161)

### Discrepancies

The number of toes on Yoda's feet has long been debated. In *[Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Absolutely_Everything_You_Need_to_Know "Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know")*, Yoda is given as having three toes at the front of each of his feet, and one at the back, comparing them with that of many birds.[[24]](#cite_note-AEYNK-24)

### Non-canon content

On October 29, 2014, for a Halloween-themed update, a costume of Yoda was added to [*The Sims 4*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Sims_4 "wikipedia:The Sims 4") for playable child Sims to wear in-game. The costume is purely cosmetic and offers no gameplay changes.[[162]](#cite_note-Sims_4-162)

[↑](#cite_ref-HRA_12_34-0) [*The High Republic Adventures* (2021) 12](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2021)_12 "The High Republic Adventures (2021) 12") 35. [↑](#cite_ref-HRA_1_date_35-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of *[The High Republic: Light of the Jedi](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Light_of_the_Jedi "The High Republic: Light of the Jedi")* to [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY"). Because one of these events is the Emergences, the events of [*The High Republic Adventures* (2021) 1](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2021)_1 "The High Republic Adventures (2021) 1") must take place at the same time as *Light of the Jedi* because it also depicts the Emergences. Therefore, because Qort is a Jedi in *The High Republic Adventures* 1, the flashbacks of [*The High Republic Adventures* (2021) 10](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2021)_10 "The High Republic Adventures (2021) 10") take place before 232 BBY because they depict Qort before he joined the Jedi. 36. [↑](#cite_ref-THRA_10_36-0) [*The High Republic Adventures* (2021) 10](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2021)_10 "The High Republic Adventures (2021) 10") 37. ↑ [37.0](#cite_ref-HRA_1_37-0) [37.1](#cite_ref-HRA_1_37-1) [37.2](#cite_ref-HRA_1_37-2) [37.3](#cite_ref-HRA_1_37-3) [37.4](#cite_ref-HRA_1_37-4) [37.5](#cite_ref-HRA_1_37-5) [*The High Republic Adventures* (2021) 1](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2021)_1 "The High Republic Adventures (2021) 1") 38. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_38-0) The [second season](/wiki/Young_Jedi_Adventures_Season_Two "Young Jedi Adventures Season Two") of *[Star Wars: Young Jedi Adventures](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Young_Jedi_Adventures "Star Wars: Young Jedi Adventures")* spans the [dedication of the Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Dedication_of_the_Starlight_Beacon "Dedication of the Starlight Beacon") (which appears in the season one finale "[The Prince and the Pirate](/wiki/The_Prince_and_the_Pirate "The Prince and the Pirate")") and the [mission to Vrant Tarnum](/wiki/Mission_to_Vrant_Tarnum "Mission to Vrant Tarnum") (which appears in "[Yoda Rescue](/wiki/Yoda_Rescue "Yoda Rescue")"), both of which are dated to [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY") by *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. The Season Two episodes "[The Great Gomgourd Quest](/wiki/The_Great_Gomgourd_Quest "The Great Gomgourd Quest")" and "[The Missing Life Day Feast](/wiki/The_Missing_Life_Day_Feast "The Missing Life Day Feast")" take place one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the [Season One](/wiki/Young_Jedi_Adventures_Season_One "Young Jedi Adventures Season One") episodes "[The Harvest Feast](/wiki/The_Harvest_Feast "The Harvest Feast")" and "[Life Day](/wiki/Life_Day_(episode) "Life Day (episode)")," placing those episodes in [233 BBY](/wiki/233_BBY "233 BBY"). Season One begins around the same year, meaning that *Young Jedi Adventures* Season One spans c. 233 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") through 232 BBY. 39. I consulted with @ahmedbest about martial arts & anime, I studied the action in "Swordsman II" (1992) in particular, I referred to Glen's dynamic drawings and I supervised the gifted animator @timanimator" ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220207192122/https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo/status/1411905860196921344)) 154. [↑](#cite_ref-Yoda_sad_154-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) Rob Coleman ([@ArfKeldo](https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo/status/1500571447450021888)): ""Acting is always the hardest part." Watching this interchange between George Lucas and me, from 20 years ago, reminds me of how much fun I had working with him. Animation is a collaborative and iterative process. We were striving for subtle nuance in the performance." ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220308030229/https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo/status/1500571447450021888)) 155. [↑](#cite_ref-Yoda_strain_155-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) Rob Coleman ([@ArfKeldo](https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo/status/1427736555246870530)): "That shot was animated by Tim Harrington @timanimator His blocking was excellent, but I was looking for more strain in Yoda's face. What are the micro-movements in one's face which illustrate that? I hung from a staircase; real pain & expression so we could study it for reference" ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220118193352/https://twitter.com/ArfKeldo/status/1427736555246870530)) 156.
